\section{Basic relations}
\subsection{periodic functions and Fourier transformations}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\sum_R e^{-igR} & = &\\
& = & \lim_{L \rightarrow \infty} \frac{e^{iGLa}(1-e^{-ig(2L+1)a})}{1-e^{-iGa}}\\
& = & \lim_{L \rightarrow \infty} \frac{e^{iG(L+1/2)a}-e^{-ig(L+1/2)a}}{e^{iGa/2}-e^{-iGa/2}}\\
& = & \lim_{L \rightarrow \infty} \frac{\sin(G(L+1/2)a}{\sin(Ga/2)}\\
\end{eqnarray*}
\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \lim_{L\rightarrow\infty}\int_{-\frac{\pi}{a}}^{\frac{\pi}{a}}\frac{\sin(GLa)}{\sin(Ga/2)} dG\\
 & = & \lim_{L\rightarrow\infty}\frac{1}{La}\int_{-L\pi}^{L\pi}\frac{\sin(GLa)}{\sin(GLa/(2L))} d(GLa)\\
 & = & \lim_{L\rightarrow\infty}\frac{1}{La}\int_{-L\pi}^{L\pi}\frac{\sin(x)}{\sin(\frac{x}{2L})} dx\\
 & = & \lim_{L\rightarrow\infty}\frac{1}{La}\int_{-L\pi}^{L\pi}\frac{\sin(x)}{\frac{x}{2L}} dx\\
 & = & \lim_{L\rightarrow\infty}\frac{2}{a}\int_{-L\pi}^{L\pi}\frac{\sin(x)}{x} dx\\
 & = & \frac{2\pi}{a}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 \sum_\mathbf{R} e^{-i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{R}} &=& \frac{(2 \pi)^3}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G}\delta(\mathbf{g} - \mathbf{G})\\
Comb(\mathbf{r}; \mathbf{R}) &:=& \sum_{\mathbf{R}} \delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})\\
{\cal F}[Comb(\mathbf{r}; \mathbf{R})] &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{V}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\\
f(\mathbf{r}) &=& Comb(\mathbf{r}; \mathbf{R})\ast f_{cell}(\mathbf{r})\\
f(\mathbf{g}) &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{V}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})f_{cell}(\mathbf{g})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
f_{cell}(r) &=& f(\mathbf{r}) ; \mathbf{r} \in V\\
 &=& 0 ; \mathbf{r} \notin V\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
f_{cell}(\mathbf{g}) &=& \int d\mathbf{r} f_{cell}(\mathbf{r})e^{-i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{r}}\\
 &=& \int_{V} d\mathbf{r} f_{cell}(\mathbf{r})e^{-i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{r}}\\
 &=& \frac{V}{N_r}\sum_{\mathbf{r}} f_{cell}(\mathbf{r})e^{-i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{r}}\\
\frac{1}{V}f_{cell}(\mathbf{g}) &=& \frac{1}{N_r}\sum_{\mathbf{r}} f_{cell}(\mathbf{r})e^{-i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{r}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
f(\mathbf{r}) &=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{g} f(\mathbf{g})e^{i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{r}}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G} f_{cell}(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\int_V f(\mathbf{r})g(\mathbf{r}) d\mathbf{r} &=&\\
&=& \int_V \frac{1}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G} f_{cell}(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} \frac{1}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G'} g_{cell}(\mathbf{G'})e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r}} d\mathbf{r}\\
&=& \frac{1}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G} f_{cell}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G'} g_{cell}(\mathbf{G'})\delta_{\mathbf{-G}, \mathbf{G'}}V\\
&=& \frac{1}{V}\sum_\mathbf{G} f_{cell}(\mathbf{G}) g_{cell}(\mathbf{-G})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{spherical harmonics and Fourier transformations}

\begin{eqnarray*}
e^{-\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}} &=& \sum_l C_l(kr)P_l(\hat{\mathbf{k}}\cdot\hat{\mathbf{r}})\\
\int_{-1}^1 e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}} P_l(\hat{\mathbf{k}}\cdot\hat{\mathbf{r}}) d(\hat{\mathbf{k}}\cdot\hat{\mathbf{r}}) &=& C_l(kr)\frac{2}{2l+1}\\
&=& 2(-i)^l j_l(kr)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

参考: 岩波 公式集III P185
\begin{equation}
j_n(z) = \frac{1}{2i^n}\int_{-1}^1 e^{izt} P_n(t)dt
\end{equation}
 
\begin{eqnarray*}
C_l(kr) = (2l+1)(-i)^l j_l(kr)\\
e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}} = \sum_l (2l+1)(-i)^l j_l(kr) P_l(\hat{\mathbf{k}}\cdot\hat{\mathbf{r}})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
P_l(\hat{\mathbf{k}}\cdot\hat{\mathbf{r}}) = \frac{4\pi}{2l+1}\sum_mY_l^{m\ast}(\hat{\mathbf{r}})Y_l^m(\hat{\mathbf{k}})
\end{equation}

参考: J.J. Sakurai 2巻 p549または岩波公式集III p137
\begin{eqnarray*}
\hat{\mathbf{r}} &=& (\sin\alpha,0,\cos\alpha)\\
\hat{\mathbf{k}} &=& (\sin\beta\cos\theta,\sin\beta\sin\theta,\cos\beta)\\
\hat{\mathbf{r}}\cdot\hat{\mathbf{k}} &=& \sin\alpha\sin\beta\cos\theta+\cos\alpha\cos\beta
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}} = \sum_l 4\pi(-i)^l j_l(kr) \sum_mY_l^{m\ast}(\hat{\mathbf{r}})Y_l^m(\hat{\mathbf{k}})
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\int f(r)Y_l^m(\hat{\mathbf{r}})e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}} d\mathbf{r}\\
&=& \int f(r)Y_l^m(\hat{\mathbf{r}})\sum_{l'} 4\pi(-i)^{l'} j_{l'}(kr) \sum_{m'}Y_{l'}^{m'\ast}(\hat{\mathbf{r}})Y_{l'}^{m'}(\hat{\mathbf{k}}) d\mathbf{r}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
\int d\hat{\mathbf{r}} Y_l^{m\ast}(\hat{\mathbf{r}})Y_{l'}^{m'}(\hat{\mathbf{r}}) = \delta_{l,l'}\delta_{m,m'}
\end{equation}

\begin{equation}
\int f(r)Y_{l}^{m}(\hat{\mathbf{r}})e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}}d\mathbf{r} = Y_{l}^{m}(\hat{\mathbf{k}})4\pi(-i)^{l}\int dr r^2 j_{l}(kr)f(r)
\end{equation}

\subsection{k-point sampling}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\langle A\rangle & = &\frac{1}{h}\int{dq}{dp}A(p)\\
& = &\int{dq}{d\frac{p}{h}}A(p)\\
& = &\int{dq}{d\frac{k}{2\pi}}A(p)\\
& = &\frac{1}{2\pi}\int{dq}{dk}A(k)\\
& = &\frac{1}{2\pi}N_{L}\int_L{dq}\int{dk}A(k)\\
\frac{1}{N_L}\langle A\rangle& = &\frac{1}{2\pi}\int_L{dq}\int{dk}A(k)\\
\langle A\rangle_{cell}& = &\frac{L}{2\pi}\int{dk}A(k)\\
\langle A\rangle_{cell}& = &\frac{1}{2\pi}\frac{\frac{2\pi}{L}}{N_{cell}}\sum_{k}\int_L{dq}A(k)\\
& = &\frac{1}{L N_{cell}}\sum_{k}\int_L{dq}A(k)\\
& = &\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{k}A(k)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

したがって三次元なら、

\begin{eqnarray*}
\langle A\rangle_{cell}& = &\frac{\Omega}{(2\pi)^3}\int{d\mathbf{k}}A(\mathbf{k})\\
& = & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}A(\mathbf{k})\\
\end{eqnarray*}
$\mathbf{k}_r = \frac{a}{2\pi}\mathbf{k}$とすると、$0\le\mathbf{k}_r\le1$であり
\[
\langle A\rangle_{cell} = \int{d\mathbf{k}_r}A(\mathbf{k}_r)\\
\]
となる。つまりブリュアンゾーンを1で規格化すると係数はでない。

\begin{eqnarray*}
\Psi_{k}(r) &=& e^{ikr}u_{k}(r)\\
u_k(r+R) &=& u_{k}(r)\\
\Psi_{k}(r+N_{cell} R) &=& \Psi_{k}(r)\\
k &=& \frac{2\pi n}{N_{cell} R}; n = 0\cdots N_{cell}\\
\int_{N_{cell} R}\Psi^\ast_k(r)\Psi_k(r)dr &=& 1\\
 &=& \int_{N_{cell} R}u^\ast_{k}(r)u_{k}(r) dr\\
 &=& N_{cell}\int_{R}u^\ast_{k}(r)u_{k}(r) dr\\
\int_{R}u^\ast_{k}(r)u_{k}(r) dr &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}} \\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
u_{k}(r) &=& \frac{1}{\sqrt{N_{cell} R}}\sum_G \phi_k(G)e^{iGr}\\
\int_{R}u^\ast_{k}(r)u_{k}(r) dr &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell} R}\sum_{G,G'} \phi^\ast_k(G)\phi_k(G')\int_R e^{-iGr}e^{iG'r} dr\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell} R}\sum_{G,G'} \phi^\ast_k(G)\phi(G')\delta_{G,G'}R\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{G} \phi^\ast_k(G)\phi(G)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
& &\langle A\rangle\\
&=&\sum_k\int_{N_{cell} R}drdr'\Psi^\ast_k(r)A(r,r')\Psi_k(r')\\
&=&\sum_k\int_{N_{cell} R}drdr'u^\ast_{k}(r)e^{-ikr}A(r,r')e^{ikr'}u_{k}(r')\\
&=&\sum_k\int_{N_{cell} R}drdr'\frac{1}{\sqrt{N_{cell} R}}\sum_{G}\phi^\ast_{k}(G)e^{-iGr}e^{-ikr}A(r,r')e^{ikr'}\frac{1}{\sqrt{N_{cell} R}}\sum_{G'}\phi_{k}(G')e^{iG'r'}\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} R}\sum_k\sum_{G,G'}\phi^\ast_{k}(G)\left[\int_{N_{cell} R}drdr'e^{-i(k+G)r}A(r,r')e^{i(k+G')r'}\right]\phi_{k}(G')\\
\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\langle A\rangle & = & \frac{1}{N_{cell} R}\sum_k\sum_{G,G'}\phi^\ast_{k}(G)\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} R}drdr'e^{-i(k+G)r}A(r,r')e^{i(k+G')r'}\right]\phi_{k}(G')\\
\end{eqnarray*}
\[A(r,r') = \delta(r,r')A(r); A(r+R) = A(r)\]
\begin{eqnarray*}
\langle A\rangle&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} R}\sum_k\sum_{G,G'}\phi^\ast_{k}(G)\left[\int_{N_{cell} R}dr e^{-i(k+G)r}A(r)e^{i(k+G')r}\right]\phi_{k}(G')\\
\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\langle A\rangle&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} R}\sum_k\sum_{G,G'}\phi^\ast_{k}(G)\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} R}dr e^{-i(k+G)r}A(r)e^{i(k+G')r}\right]\phi_{k}(G')\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\newpage

\subsection{fermi面積分}

xTAPPの$\cos$展開によるfermi面積分の詳細

\[
 \int_{k; e(k)<E_f} \cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k}
\]
の計算について。

\begin{enumerate}
\item 一旦、第一ブリュアンゾーンを格子分割する
\item 格子分割でできる、各セルについて考える
\begin{enumerate}
\item セルの頂点全部が$E_f$以下であれば、そのセルについての積分は厳密に行う。セルが平行６面体なので、厳密に計算できる。
\item セルの頂点が部分的に$E_f$以下になる場合、このセルを4面体分割して4面体法で積分を行う。
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}

全部を四面体分割で計算していないことに注意。四面体分割で計算されているのはフェルミ面付近
だけである。

\newpage

\subsection{symmetry operations}

$\mathcal{T}$: operation acts on objects (not on coordinates).
$\mathcal{T}$ consists of a rotation by $\mathrm{T}$ followed by a
translation by $\mathbf{p}$.

\[ \mathcal{T}[f(\mathbf{r})] = f(\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathbf{r - p})) \]

Fourier transformation.

\[ f(\mathbf{r}) = \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G}f(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\cdot\mathbf{r}} \]

\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{T}[f(\mathbf{r})] &=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\cdot [\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathbf{r} - \mathbf{p})]}\\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G})e^{i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot [(\mathbf{r} - \mathbf{p})]} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G})e^{i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{r}} e^{-i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{p}} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{p}} e^{i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{r}} \\
\end{eqnarray*}

in cell coordinate $\mathbf{r}_c$, where $\mathbf{r} = \mathrm{A}\mathbf{r}_c$,
$\mathbf{G}_c = \mathrm{A}^t\mathbf{G}$

\[\mathbf{G}\cdot\mathbf{r} = \mathbf{G}\cdot(\mathrm{A}\mathbf{r}_c) = (\mathrm{A}^t\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}_c = \mathbf{G}_c\cdot\mathbf{r}_c \]

\[ f(\mathbf{r}) = f(\mathrm{A}\mathbf{r_c}) = f_c(\mathbf{r_c}) \]

\begin{eqnarray*}
T[f_c(\mathbf{r}_c)] &=& T[f(\mathrm{A}\mathbf{r_c})] \\
&=&f(\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathrm{A}\mathbf{r_c} - \mathbf{p}))\\
&=&f_c(\mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathrm{A}\mathbf{r_c} - \mathbf{p}))\\
&=&f_c( (\mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathrm{T}^{-1}\mathrm{A})(\mathbf{r_c} - \mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathbf{p}))\\
&=&f_c( \mathrm{T}_c^{-1}(\mathbf{r_c} - \mathbf{p}_c))\\
\end{eqnarray*}
where, $\mathrm{T}_c = \mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathrm{T}\mathrm{A}$ and $p_c = \mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathbf{p}$

\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{T}[f(\mathbf{r})] &=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot (\mathrm{A}\mathbf{p}_c)} e^{i[(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot (\mathrm{A}\mathbf{r}_c)} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[\mathrm{A}^t(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{p}_c} e^{i[\mathrm{A}^t(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{r}_c} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[\mathrm{A}^t(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t(\mathrm{A}^t)^{-1}\mathrm{A}^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{p}_c} e^{i[\mathrm{A}^t(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t(\mathrm{A}^t)^{-1}\mathrm{A}^t\mathbf{G}]\cdot\mathbf{r}_c} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[\mathrm{A}^t(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t(\mathrm{A}^t)^{-1}\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{p}_c} e^{i[\mathrm{A}^t(\mathrm{T}^{-1})^t(\mathrm{A}^t)^{-1}\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{r}_c} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[(\mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathrm{T}^{-1}\mathrm{A})^t\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{p}_c} e^{i[(\mathrm{A}^{-1}\mathrm{T}^{-1}\mathrm{A})^t\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{r}_c} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[(\mathrm{T_c}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{p}_c} e^{i[(\mathrm{T_c}^{-1})^t\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{r}_c} \\
&=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G} f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{p}_c} e^{i[\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c]\cdot\mathbf{r}_c} \\
\end{eqnarray*}
where, $\mathrm{S}_c = (\mathrm{T}_c^{-1})^t$ and $\mathrm{T}_c = (\mathrm{S}_c^t)^{-1}$.

namely, by the transformation
\[
 \mathbf{G}_c \rightarrow \mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c
\]
\[
 A^t\mathbf{G} \rightarrow \mathrm{S_c}A^t\mathbf{G}
\]
\[
 \mathbf{G} \rightarrow (A^t)^{-1}\mathrm{S_c}A^t\mathbf{G} = S \mathbf{G}
\]
where, 
\[
S = (A^t)^{-1}\mathrm{S_c}A^t = (A^t)^{-1}(\mathrm{T_c}^{-1})^tA^t = (((A^{-1}\mathrm{T_c}A)^{-1})^t = (T^{-1})^t
\]

\[
 f(\mathbf{G}) \ @ \ \mathbf{G}_c \rightarrow f(\mathbf{G})e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c\cdot\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @ \ \mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c
\]

\subsubsection{multiplication}
By $\mathcal{T}_2\left[\mathcal{T}_1\left[f(\mathbf{r})]\right]\right]$
\begin{eqnarray*}
 f(\mathbf{G}) \ @ \ \mathbf{G}_c & \rightarrow & f(\mathbf{G})e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c^1\cdot\mathrm{S_c^1}\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @ \ \mathrm{S_c^1}\mathbf{G}_c \\
 & \rightarrow & f(\mathbf{G})e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c^1\cdot\mathrm{S_c^1}\mathbf{G}_c]}e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c^2\cdot\mathrm{S_c^2}\mathrm{S_c^1}\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @ \ \mathrm{S_c^2}\mathrm{S_c^1}\mathbf{G}_c \\
  &=& f(\mathbf{G})e^{-i\left[(\mathbf{p}_c^{1})^t\mathrm{S_c^1}+(\mathbf{p}_c^2)^t\mathrm{S_c^2}\mathrm{S_c^1}\right]\mathbf{G}_c} \ @ \ \mathrm{S_c^2}\mathrm{S_c^1}\mathbf{G}_c 
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsubsection{inversion}
Inverse operation is translation by $-\mathbf{p}_c$ followed by rotation by $\mathrm{S_c^{-1}}$.
\begin{eqnarray*}
 f(\mathbf{G}) \ @ \ \mathbf{G}_c & \rightarrow & f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[-\mathbf{p}_c\cdot\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @ \ \mathbf{G}_c \\
 & \rightarrow & f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[-\mathbf{p}_c\cdot\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @ \ \mathrm{S_c^{-1}}\mathbf{G}_c \\
 & = & f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[(-\mathrm{S_c}^t\mathbf{p}_c)\cdot (\mathrm{S_c^{-1}}\mathbf{G}_c)]} \ @ \ \mathrm{S_c^{-1}}\mathbf{G}_c \\
\end{eqnarray*}

This means rotation by $\mathrm{S_c^{-1}}$ followed by translation by $-\mathrm{S_c}^t\mathbf{p}_c$.

\subsection{time reversal symmetry}

Suppose Hamiltonian $H$ is a real operator. Namely $H^\ast = H$.

Then
\begin{eqnarray*}
 H\Psi_\mathbf{k} &=& e(\mathbf{k}) \Psi_\mathbf{k}\\
 H^\ast\Psi^\ast_\mathbf{k} &=& e(\mathbf{k})\Psi^\ast_\mathbf{k}\\
 H\Psi^\ast_\mathbf{k} &=& e(\mathbf{k})\Psi^\ast_\mathbf{k}\\
\end{eqnarray*}
Namely, $\Psi^\ast_\mathbf{k}$ is a eigen function whose eigen energy is $e(\mathbf{k})$.
\[
 \Psi(\mathbf{k}) = e^{i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{r}}u_\mathbf{k}(\mathbf{r}),
\]
where
\[
 u_\mathbf{k}(\mathbf{r}+\mathbf{R}) = u_\mathbf{k}(\mathbf{r}),
\]
for any lattice vector $\mathbf{R}$.
\[
 \Psi^\ast(\mathbf{k}) = e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{r}}u^\ast_\mathbf{k}(\mathbf{r})
\]
Because
\[
 \Psi^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{R}) = e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{r}}e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}}u^\ast_\mathbf{k}(\mathbf{r}+\mathbf{R}) = e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}}e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{r}}u^\ast_\mathbf{k}(\mathbf{r}) = e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}}\Psi^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{R})
\]
$\Psi^\ast(\mathbf{k})$ is a eigen function on $-\mathbf{k}$.
Namely, $e(\mathbf{k}) = e(-\mathbf{k})$.

\subsection{time reversal and space group symmetry operation}

$\mathcal{T}$: operation acts on objects (not on coordinates).
$\mathcal{T}$ consists of a rotation by $\mathrm{T}$ followed by a
translation by $\mathbf{p}$.

\[ \mathcal{T}[f(\mathbf{r})] = f(\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathbf{r - p})) \]

$\mathcal{O}$: time reversal operation

\[ \mathcal{O}[f(\mathbf{r})] = f(\mathbf{r})^\ast \]

\[
  \mathcal{O}[\mathcal{T}[f(\mathbf{r})]] = \mathcal{O}[f(\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathbf{r - p})) = f(\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathbf{r - p}))^\ast
\]
\[
  \mathcal{T}[\mathcal{O}[f(\mathbf{r})]] = \mathcal{T}[f(\mathbf{r})^\ast] = f(\mathrm{T}^{-1}(\mathbf{r - p}))^\ast
\]

$\mathcal{T}$ and $\mathcal{O}$ are commutable.

\[ \mathcal{O}[f(\mathbf{r})] = f(\mathbf{r})^\ast = \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G}f(\mathbf{G})^\ast e^{-i\mathbf{G}\cdot\mathbf{r}} = \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G}f(\mathbf{G})^\ast e^{i(-\mathbf{G}_c)\cdot\mathbf{r}_c}\]

Namely, by $\mathcal{O}$,
\[
 f(\mathbf{G}) \ @\  \mathbf{G}_c \rightarrow f(\mathbf{G})^\ast \ @\  -\mathbf{G}_c
\]

By $\mathcal{O}\mathcal{T}$,
\begin{eqnarray*}
 f(\mathbf{G}) \ @\ \mathbf{G}_c \ &\rightarrow& f(\mathbf{G}) e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c\cdot\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @\ \mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c \\
 & \rightarrow & f(\mathbf{G})^\ast e^{i[\mathbf{p}_c\cdot \mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c]} \ @\ -\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c \\
 & = & f(\mathbf{G})^\ast e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c\cdot (-\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c)]} \ @\ -\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c
\end{eqnarray*}

By $\mathcal{T}\mathcal{O}$,
\begin{eqnarray*}
 f(\mathbf{G}) \ @\ \mathbf{G}_c \ &\rightarrow& f(\mathbf{G})^\ast \ @\ -\mathbf{G}_c \ \\
 &\rightarrow& f(\mathbf{G})^\ast e^{-i[\mathbf{p}_c\cdot (-\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c)]} \ @\ -\mathrm{S_c}\mathbf{G}_c \\
\end{eqnarray*}

This also means that $\mathcal{T}$ and $\mathcal{O}$ are commutable.

\subsection{symmetry operation on strain tensor}
$c$: strain tensor.

\begin{eqnarray*}
  [\mathcal{T}c]_{ij} &=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{\partial (T\mathbf{u}(T^{-1}(r-p)))_i}{\partial r_j} + \frac{\partial (T\mathbf{u}(T^{-1}(r-p)))_j}{\partial r_i}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{\partial (T\mathbf{u}(T^{-1}r))_i}{\partial r_j} + \frac{\partial (T\mathbf{u}(T^{-1}r))_j}{\partial r_i}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{\partial (T\mathbf{u}(T^{-1}r))_i}{\partial (T^{-1}r)_k}\frac{\partial (T^{-1}r)_k}{\partial r_j} + \frac{\partial (T\mathbf{u}(T^{-1}r))_j}{\partial (T^{-1}r)_k}\frac{\partial (T^{-1}r)_k}{\partial r_i}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{(T\partial\mathbf{u})_i}{\partial r_k}T^{-1}_{kj} + \frac{(T\partial\mathbf{u})_j}{\partial r_k}T^{-1}_{ki}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{T_{im}\partial u_m}{\partial r_k}T^{-1}_{kj} + \frac{T_{jm}\partial u_m}{\partial r_k}T^{-1}_{ki}\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}
$T$ is a orthogonal transformation. $T^{-1}_{ij} = T_{ji}$.
\begin{eqnarray*}
  [\mathcal{T}c]_{ij}&=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{T_{im}\partial u_m}{\partial r_k}T^{-1}_{kj} + \frac{T^{-1}_{mj}\partial u_m}{\partial r_k}T_{ik}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{T_{im}\partial u_m}{\partial r_k}T^{-1}_{kj} + \frac{T^{-1}_{kj}\partial u_k}{\partial r_m}T_{im}\right)\\
  &=& T_{im}\frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{\partial u_m}{\partial r_k} + \frac{\partial u_k}{\partial r_m}\right)T^{-1}_{kj}\\
  &=& T_{im}c_{mk}T^{-1}_{kj}\\
  &=& T_{im}c_{mk}T_{jk}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{symmetry operation on stress tensor}
$c, \sigma$: strain tensor and stress tensor.

\begin{eqnarray*}
  [\mathcal{T}\sigma]_{ij} &=& \frac{\partial{E_{total}[\mathcal{T}c]}}{\partial c_{ij}}\\
  &=& \frac{\partial{E_{total}[\mathcal{T}c]}}{\partial (\mathcal{T}c)_{mk}}\frac{\partial (\mathcal{T}c)_{mk}}{\partial T_{ij}}\\
  &=& \frac{\partial{E_{total}}}{\partial c_{mk}}\frac{\partial T_{mp}c_{pq}T_{kq}}{\partial c_{ij}}\\
  &=& \frac{\partial{E_{total}}}{\partial c_{mk}}T_{mp}\delta_{pi}\delta_{qj}T_{kq}\\
  &=& \frac{\partial{E_{total}}}{\partial c_{mk}}T_{mi}T_{kj}\\
  &=& T_{mi}\sigma_{mk}T_{kj}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{symmetry averaging of charge distribution}
\begin{description}
  \item[$\hat{Q}(r)$:] operator to give charge distribition at position $r$

  \item[$T_i$ and $T$:] a symmetry operator and its group for a system

  \item[$S_j(k)$ and $S(k)$:] a symmetry operator conserve a irreducible k point and its group

  \item[$R(k)$ and $R_i(k)$:] an irreducible sub set of $T$ which generates $T$ from $S(k)$ and an operator in it
\end{description}
 
\begin{eqnarray*}
  & &  \sum_{kn}\langle\psi_{kn}|\hat{Q}(r)|\psi_{kn}\rangle\\
  &=& \sum_{k;\mathrm{irr}} \sum_{i;R(k)}\sum_n\langle\psi_{kn}|R_i^\dag(k) \hat{Q}(r) R_i(k)|\psi_{kn}\rangle\\
  &=& \sum_{k;\mathrm{irr}} \sum_{i;R(k)}\sum_n\langle\psi_{kn}|[R_i(k)\hat{Q}](r)|\psi_{kn}\rangle\\
  &=& \sum_{k;\mathrm{irr}} \sum_{i;R(k)} R_i(k)[ \rho_k(r) ]\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\[
 \rho_k(r) = \sum_n\langle\psi_{kn}|\hat{Q}(r)|\psi_{kn}\rangle
\]
is invariant under $S(k)$. Therefore,
\begin{eqnarray*}
  &=& \sum_{kn}\langle\psi_{kn}|\hat{Q}(r)|\psi_{kn}\rangle\\
  &=& \sum_{k;\mathrm{irr}} \sum_{i;R(k)} R_i(k) \frac{1}{|S(k)|} \sum_{j;S(k)} S_j(k) [\rho_k(r)]\\
  &=& \sum_{k;\mathrm{irr}} \frac{1}{|S(k)|} \sum_{i;R(k)}\sum_{j;S(k)} R_i(k)S_j(k)[\rho_k(r)]\\
\end{eqnarray*}

Because $R(k)S(k) = T$ and $|T| = |S(k)| \cdot |R(k)|$,
\begin{eqnarray*}
  &=& \sum_{k;irr} \frac{1}{|S(k)|} \sum_{i;T}T_i[ \rho_k(r) ]\\
  &=&  \sum_{i;T}T_i\left[ \sum_{k;irr} \frac{1}{|S(k)|}\rho_k(r) \right]\\
  &=& \frac{1}{|T|} \sum_{i;T}T_i\left[ \sum_{k;irr} |R(k)| \rho_k(r) \right]
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{symmetry operation on eigen energy}

eigen energy of the wave function and its cos expansion.

\[
 e(\mathbf{k}) = \sum_\mathbf{R}c(\mathbf{R})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})
\]
where, $c(\mathbf{R}) = c(-\mathbf{R})$.

\[
 H\psi(\mathbf{k}) = e(\mathbf{k})\psi(\mathbf{k})
\]

$\mathcal{T}$: symmetry operation.

$H$ is invaliant under $\mathcal{T}$.
\[
 H\mathcal{T} = \mathcal{T}H, \mathcal{T}^{-1}H\mathcal{T} = H
\]

\[
 \mathcal{T}^{-1}H\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}) = e(\mathbf{k})\psi(\mathbf{k})
\]
\[
 H\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}) = e(\mathbf{k})\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k})
\]
$\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k})$ has the same eigen value $e(\mathbf{k})$.

For real lattice vector $\mathbf{R}$,
\[
 \psi(\mathbf{k}; r+\mathbf{R})= e^{i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r)
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
 \mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r+\mathbf{R}) &=& \mathcal{T}\sum_\mathbf{G}c(\mathbf{G})e^{i(\mathbf{k+G})\cdot(\mathbf{r+R})}\\
 &=& \mathcal{T}\sum_{\mathbf{G}_c}c(\mathbf{G}_c)e^{i(\mathbf{k}_c+\mathbf{G}_c)\cdot(\mathbf{r}_c+\mathbf{R}_c)}\\
 &=& \sum_{\mathbf{G}_c}c(\mathbf{G}_c)e^{-i(S_c\mathbf{k}_c+S_c\mathbf{G}_c)\cdot\mathbf{p}_c}e^{i(S_c\mathbf{k}_c+S_c\mathbf{G}_c)\cdot(\mathbf{r}_c+\mathbf{R}_c)}\\
 &=& e^{iS_c\mathbf{k}_c\cdot\mathbf{R}_c}\sum_{\mathbf{G}_c}c(\mathbf{G}_c)e^{-i(S_c\mathbf{k}_c+S_c\mathbf{G}_c)\cdot\mathbf{p}_c}e^{i(S_c\mathbf{k}_c+S_c\mathbf{G}_c)\cdot\mathbf{r}_c}\\
 &=& e^{iS_c\mathbf{k}_c\cdot\mathbf{R}_c}\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r)\\
 &=& e^{iA^t(A^t)^{-1}S_cA^t(A^t)^{-1}\mathbf{k}_c\cdot\mathbf{R}_c}\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r)\\
 &=& e^{i(A^t)^{-1}S_cA^t(A^t)^{-1}\mathbf{k}_c\cdot A\mathbf{R}_c}\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r)\\
 &=& e^{i(S\mathbf{k})\cdot \mathbf{R}}\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

Therefore, $\mathcal{T}\psi(\mathbf{k}; r)$ is a wave function on k point, $S\mathbf{k}$. This means $e(S\mathbf{k}) = e(\mathbf{k})$.

Now

\begin{eqnarray*}
 \int_{BZ} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k} &=& \sum_{\mathbf{R}'}c(\mathbf{R}')\int_{BZ}\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}')\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})d\mathbf{k}\\
&=& c(0)\int_{BZ}\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})d\mathbf{k} + 
\sum_{\textrm{one of }\mathbf{R}', -\mathbf{R}'}2c(\mathbf{R}')\int_{BZ}\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}')\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})d\mathbf{k}\\
&=& c(0)\delta_{\mathbf{R},0}V_{BZ} + 
\sum_{\textrm{one of }\mathbf{R}', -\mathbf{R}'}c(\mathbf{R}')\delta_{\mathbf{R}',\mathbf{R}}V_{BZ}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

Therefore,
\[
 c(\mathbf{R}) = \frac{1}{V_{BZ}}\int_{BZ} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k}
\]

\begin{description}
  \item[$S_i$ and $S$:] a symmetry operator and its group for a system

  \item[$\tilde{S}_j(k)$ and $\tilde{S}(k)$:] a symmetry operator conserve a irreducible k point and its group

  \item[$\hat{S}(k)$ and $\hat{S}_i(k)$:] an irreducible sub set of $S$ which generates $S$ from $\tilde{S}(k)$ and an operator in it
\end{description}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 c(\mathbf{R}) &\sim& \frac{1}{V_{BZ}} \sum_{\mathbf{k}; \textrm{sampled}} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) \frac{V_{BZ}}{N_k}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{N_k} \sum_{\mathbf{k}; \textrm{sampled}} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})\\
 &=& \frac{1}{N_k} \sum_{\mathbf{k}; irr}\sum_{i;\hat{S}(\mathbf{k})} e(\hat{S}_i(\mathbf{k})\mathbf{k})\cos(\hat{S}_i(\mathbf{k})\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})\\
 &=& \frac{1}{N_k} \sum_{\mathbf{k}; irr}e(\mathbf{k})\sum_{i;\hat{S}(\mathbf{k})} \cos(\hat{S}_i(\mathbf{k})\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

$T$ matrices acting on real grid deduced from $S$ symmetry matrices.
\begin{description}
  \item[$T_i$ and $T$:] symmetry matrices acting on real grid.

  \item[$\tilde{T}_j(R)$ and $\tilde{T}(R)$:] a symmetry operator conserve a irreducible $R$ point and its group

 \item[$\hat{T}(R)$ and $\hat{T}_i(R)$:] an irreducible sub set of $T$ which generates $T$ from $\tilde{T}(R)$ and an operator in it
\end{description}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 c(T\mathbf{R}) &=& \frac{1}{V_{BZ}}\int_{BZ} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot T\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k}\\
&=& \frac{1}{V_{BZ}}\int_{BZ} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(S\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k}\\
&=& \frac{1}{V_{BZ}}\int_{BZ} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(S\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d(S\mathbf{k})\\
&=& \frac{1}{V_{BZ}}\int_{BZ} e(S^{-1}\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k}\\
&=& \frac{1}{V_{BZ}}\int_{BZ} e(\mathbf{k})\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}) d\mathbf{k}\\
&=& c(\mathbf{R})
\end{eqnarray*}

\[
 e(\mathbf{k}) = \sum_{\mathbf{R}; irr}c(\mathbf{R})\sum_{i; \hat{T}(\mathbf{R})}\cos(\mathbf{k}\cdot\hat{T}_i(\mathbf{R})\mathbf{R})
\]

\begin{description}
\item[\texttt{rco}:] $\sum_{i;\hat{S}(\mathbf{k})} \cos(\hat{S}_i(\mathbf{k})\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R})$, where $\mathbf{k}$,$\mathbf{R}$ are irreducible. 

\item[\texttt{nsy}:] $|\hat{T}(\mathbf{R})|$, where $\mathbf{R}$ is irreducible. 

\item[\texttt{kz}:] $\hat{T}_i(\mathbf{R})\mathbf{R}$, where $\mathbf{R}$ is irreducible.
\end{description}

\subsection{translation of wave function in $k$ space}

in cell coordinate

\[
 \psi_{k_c} = \sum_{G_c} c(G_c)e^{i(k_c+G_c)r_c}
\]
\[
 \psi_{k'_c} = \sum_{G'_c} c(G'_c)e^{i(k'_c+G'_c)r_c} 
\]

Correspoinding $G_c$ and $G'_c$ satisfy
\[
k_c + G_c + \Delta = k'_c + G'_c
\]
where $-1/2 < \Delta < 1/2$.
\[
k'_c - k_c + G'_c - G_c = \Delta
\]
\[
\mathrm{nint}(k'_c - k_c) + G'_c - G_c = 0
\]
\[
G_c = G'_c + \mathrm{nint}(k'_c - k_c)
\]

\newpage
\section{Normalization of wave-functions}

\begin{eqnarray*}
1&=&\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}\Psi_k^\ast(\mathbf{r})\left(\delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}) + \sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})\right)\Psi_k(\mathbf{r'})d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}\\
&=&\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}}u_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{r})\left(\delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}) + \sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})\right)u_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{r'})e^{i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r'}}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}\\
&=&\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}u_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{r})\left(\delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}) + \sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})e^{i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r'}}\right)u_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{r'})d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}\\
&=&\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\Bigg(\delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}) \\
&+& \sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})e^{i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r'}}\Bigg)\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G'})e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}\\
&=&\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G'})e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r}}d\mathbf{r}\\
&+& \int_{N_{cell}\Omega}\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})e^{i\mathbf{k}\mathbf{r'}}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G'})e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}\\
&=&\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G'})\delta_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\\
&+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{R}}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{R}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k}}^\ast(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\newpage
\section{Total energy per a unit cell}

\begin{eqnarray*}
H &=& H_{kinet} + H_{local} + H_{nonlocal} + H_{hartree} + H_{xc}\\
H_{kinet} &=& -\frac{1}{2}\nabla^{2}\\
H_{local} &=& \sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})\\
H_{hartree} &=& \int d\mathbf{r'}\frac{\rho(\mathbf{r'})}{|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
E_{cell} = E_{kinet} + E_{local} + E_{nonlocal} + E_{hartree} + E_{xc} + E_{ewald}
\end{equation}

\subsection{Kinetic Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{kinet} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\left(-\frac{1}{2}\nabla^{2}\right)e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}}\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\left(-\frac{1}{2}\nabla^{2}\right)e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{i(\mathbf{G'}-\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})^2\\
 &=& \int_{\Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{i(\mathbf{G'}-\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})^2\\
 &=& \frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})^2\Omega\delta_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{kinet} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})^2\Omega\delta_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Local potential Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{local;\phi} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\mathbf{r},\mathbf{R}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}}\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\mathbf{r},\mathbf{R}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}} &=&\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\mathbf{r},\mathbf{R}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})\\
&=&\int_{N_{cell} \Omega} d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\mathbf{r}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{r})\\
&=&\sum_{\tau}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega} d\mathbf{r} e^{-i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{r})\\
&=&\sum_{\tau}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{local;\phi} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{local} &=& \int_\Omega \sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}}V^\tau(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})\rho(\mathbf{r}) d\mathbf{r}\\
&=&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d\mathbf{r}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}}V^\tau(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{-G})\\
&=&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d\mathbf{r}\sum_{\tau}V^\tau(\mathbf{r})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{-G})\\
&=&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{-G})
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Charge distribution}

\begin{equation}
\rho = \rho_{\phi} + \rho_{core}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{band charge}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x}) &=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{x})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r}}\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{x}}e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{x}}\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{x}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\right]^\ast\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{x}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_\mathbf{k,\sigma,n}\Omega\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}^\ast(\mathbf{x})\Omega\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{x})\\
&=&\frac{\Omega}{N_{cell}}\sum_\mathbf{k,\sigma,n}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}^\ast(\mathbf{x})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{x})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
\int_V d\mathbf{x}\phi^\ast(\mathbf{x})\phi(\mathbf{x}) = \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast(\mathbf{G})\phi(\mathbf{G}) = \frac{1}{\Omega}
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G}) & = & \int_{\Omega}d\mathbf{x}\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\\
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G}) & = & \frac{\Omega}{N_{xyz}}\sum_{\mathbf{x}}\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\\
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G}) & = & \frac{\Omega}{N_{xyz}}\sum_{\mathbf{x}}e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'},\mathbf{G''}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})e^{-i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{x}}e^{i\mathbf{G''}\mathbf{x}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
& = & \frac{1}{N_{xyz}}\sum_{\mathbf{x}}e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'},\mathbf{G''}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})e^{-i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{x}}e^{i\mathbf{G''}\mathbf{x}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
& = & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'},\mathbf{G''}}\delta_{\mathbf{G}+\mathbf{G'},\mathbf{G''}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
& = & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}+\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsubsection{core charge}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\rho_{core}(\mathbf{x})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\\
& &\times \left[\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r'}}\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R}) & = & \int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r})\\
& = & e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{R}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r})\\
& = & e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\rho_{core}(\mathbf{x})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{R}}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}


\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\rho_{core; cell}(\mathbf{G})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\mathbf{R}}\int_\Omega d\mathbf{x}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\sum_{\mathbf{R}}\int_\Omega d\mathbf{x}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})e^{-i\mathbf{G}{x}} &=& \sum_{\mathbf{R}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega} Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x}-\mathbf{R})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}d\mathbf{x}\\
 & = & \sum_{\mathbf{R}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega} Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{R}}d\mathbf{x}\\
 & = & \sum_{\mathbf{R}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega} Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}d\mathbf{x}\\
 & = & \int_{N_{cell} \Omega} Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{x})e^{-i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}d\mathbf{x}\\
 & = & Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\rho_{core; cell}(\mathbf{G})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Hartree Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{hartree} &=& \frac{1}{2}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\int_{N_{cell}\Omega} d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'} \frac{\rho(\mathbf{r})\rho(\mathbf{r'})e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}}{|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}\\
&=& \frac{1}{2}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\int_{N_{cell}\Omega} d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'} \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{G'})e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}\frac{e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}}{|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}\\
&=& \frac{1}{2\Omega^2}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{G'})\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'} e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}\frac{e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}}{|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'} e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}\frac{e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}}{|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|} &=& \int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'})d\mathbf{r'} e^{i\mathbf{G}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}+\mathbf{r'})}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}\frac{e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}}{|\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r'}|}\\
 &=& \int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'} e^{i\mathbf{G}(\mathbf{r}+\mathbf{r'})}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{r'}}\frac{e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}|}}{|\mathbf{r}|}\\
 &=& N_{cell}\Omega\delta_{\mathbf{G},-\mathbf{G'}}\int_{N_{cell}\Omega}d\mathbf{r} e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\frac{e^{-\alpha|\mathbf{r}|}}{|\mathbf{r}|}\\
 &=& N_{cell}\Omega\delta_{\mathbf{G},-\mathbf{G'}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
E_{hartree} = \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{cell}(\mathbf{-G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}
\end{equation}

\subsection{Non-local potential Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E_{nonlocal}\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\\
& &\times \left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\int_{N_{cell} \Omega}d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^{\ast}(\mathbf{r'}-\mathbf{R})e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{r'}}\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}e^{-i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G'})\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\left[\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Ewald Energy}

\begin{equation}
E_{ewald} = \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{1}{2}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}}\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{R'}}\frac{Z_\tau Z_{\tau'}}{|\tau+\mathbf{R}-\tau'-\mathbf{R'}|}e^{-\alpha|\tau+\mathbf{R}-\tau'-\mathbf{R'}|}
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{ion}(\mathbf{r}) & := & \sum_{\mathbf{R},\tau}Z_{\tau}\delta(\mathbf{r}-\tau-\mathbf{R})\\
& = & Comb(\mathbf{r};\mathbf{R})\ast\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\delta(\mathbf{r}-\tau)\\
\rho_{ion}(\mathbf{g}) & = & \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G}) \sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}e^{-i\tau\mathbf{g}}\\
\rho_{ion;cell}(\mathbf{G}) & = & \sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}e^{-i\tau\mathbf{G}}\\
E_{ewald} &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\rho_{ion;cell}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{ion;cell}(\mathbf{-G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}e^{-i\tau\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau'}Z_{\tau'}e^{i\tau'\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\left[e^{-\gamma^2(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)}+1-e^{-\gamma^2(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)}\right]\\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}e^{-\gamma^2(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)}\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
& & \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)}\right]\\
&=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right] + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2\alpha^2}\right]\\
&=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right] + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}4\pi\gamma^2\\
&=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right]\\
&=&\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left(1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right)e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\\
&=&\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{\Omega}\frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G}(2\pi)^3Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left(1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right)e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\\
&=&\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{G}\frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left(1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right)e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\\
&=&\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\left[Comb(\mathbf{r};\mathbf{R})\ast{\cal F}^{-1}\left[\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\left(1-e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2}\right)\right]\right](\tau-\tau')\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&{\cal F}^{-1}\left[\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{g}^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2 \mathbf{g}^2}\right]\right]\\
&=&\frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int dgd(\cos\theta) 2\pi g^2\frac{4\pi}{g^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2g^2}\right]e^{igr\cos\theta}\\
&=&\frac{1}{\pi}\int dgd(\cos\theta)\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2g^2}\right]e^{igr\cos\theta}\\
&=&\frac{1}{\pi}\int dg\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2g^2}\right]\frac{1}{igr}\left[e^{igr}-e^{-igr}\right]\\
&=&\frac{2}{\pi}\int dg\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2g^2}\right]\frac{\sin(gr)}{gr}\\
&=&\frac{1}{r}-\frac{2}{\pi r}\int dge^{-\gamma^2g^2}\frac{\sin(gr)}{g}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
I(r)&=&\int dge^{-\gamma^2g^2}\frac{\sin(gr)}{g}\\
&=&\int d(gr)e^{-\frac{\gamma^2(gr)^2}{r^2}}\frac{\sin(gr)}{gr}\\
&=&\int dge^{-\frac{\gamma^2g^2}{r^2}}\frac{\sin(g)}{g}\\
I(0)&=& 0\\
\frac{dI}{dr}&=&\int dge^{-\gamma^2g^2}\cos(gr)\\
             &=&\frac{1}{2}\int_{-\infty}^{-\infty}dge^{-\gamma^2g^2}e^{igr}\\
             &=&\frac{1}{2}\int_{-\infty}^{-\infty}dge^{-\gamma^2(g-\frac{ir}{2\gamma^2})^2 - \frac{r^2}{4\gamma^2}}\\
             &=&\frac{1}{2}e^{-\frac{r^2}{4\gamma^2}}\frac{\sqrt{\pi}}{\gamma}\\
I(r)&=&\int_0^r dt\frac{1}{2}e^{-\frac{t^2}{4\gamma^2}}\frac{\sqrt{\pi}}{\gamma}\\
&=&\int_0^{\frac{r}{2\gamma}} d\left(\frac{t}{2\gamma}\right)e^{-\left(\frac{t}{2\gamma}\right)^2}\sqrt{\pi}\\
&=&\int_0^{\frac{r}{2\gamma}} dte^{-t^2}\sqrt{\pi}\\
&=&\frac{\pi}{2}\frac{2}{\sqrt{\pi}}\int_0^{\frac{r}{2\gamma}} dte^{-t^2}\\
&=&\frac{\pi}{2}\mathrm{erf}(\frac{r}{2\gamma})
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&{\cal F}^{-1}\left[\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{g}^2}\left[1-e^{-\gamma^2 \mathbf{g}^2}\right]\right]\\
&=&\frac{1}{r}-\frac{1}{r}\mathrm{erf}(\frac{r}{2\gamma})\\
&=&\frac{1}{r}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{r}{2\gamma})
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{ewald} &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}e^{-i(\tau-\tau')\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}e^{-\gamma^2(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\tau',\mathbf{R}}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}e^{-i\tau\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau'}Z_{\tau'}e^{i\tau'\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} + \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\tau,\tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2}e^{-\gamma^2\alpha^2} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\tau',\mathbf{R} (\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & + \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\tau'(\tau\ne\tau')}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & + \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau = \tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'|}\bigg[1 - \mathrm{erf}\bigg(\frac{|\tau-\tau'|}{2\gamma}\bigg)\bigg] \\
\end{eqnarray*}

Remove self interaction energy. Notice
\[
  \lim_{x\rightarrow 0}\frac{1}{x}\mathrm{erf}(ax) = \frac{1}{x}(\frac{2}{\sqrt\pi}ax + O(x^2)) = \frac{2}{\sqrt\pi}a
\]

Define
\[
S^Z(\mathbf{G}) = \sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}e^{-i\tau\mathbf{G}}
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{ewald} &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & + \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2}(1 - \gamma^2\alpha^2) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau\ne\tau',\mathbf{R} (\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R} (\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}^2\frac{1}{|\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & + \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\tau'(\tau\ne\tau')}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & - \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau = \tau'}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'|}\mathrm{erf}\bigg(\frac{|\tau-\tau'|}{2\gamma}\bigg) \\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & + \frac{1}{2\Omega}\bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2} - \frac{1}{2\Omega}\bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2 4\pi\gamma^2 \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau\ne\tau',\mathbf{R}}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R} (\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}^2\frac{1}{|\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & - \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}^2\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt{\pi}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Ewald Energy: yet another}

\begin{equation}
E_{ewald} = \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R},\tau'; \tau \ne \tau'+\mathbf{R}}\frac{Z_\tau Z_{\tau'}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}
\end{equation}

遮蔽電荷分布
\begin{eqnarray*}
  \rho_{scr}(\mathbf{r}) &=& \sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}(2\gamma)^3}\exp\left(-\frac{(\mathbf{r} - \tau - \mathbf{R})^2}{4\gamma^2}\right)\\
  &=& Comb(\mathbf{r};\mathbf{R})\ast\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}(2\gamma)^3}\exp\left(-\frac{(\mathbf{r} - \tau)^2}{4\gamma^2}\right)\right]
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
点電荷分布 = (点電荷分布 - 遮蔽電荷分布) + 遮蔽電荷分布
\end{equation}

\begin{equation}
全静電ポテンシャル = 静電ポテンシャル(点電荷分布 - 遮蔽電荷分布) + 静電ポテンシャル(遮蔽電荷分布)
\end{equation}

静電ポテンシャルを決めるポアソン方程式
\begin{equation}
  -\nabla^2\phi(r) = 4\pi\rho(r)
\end{equation}
逆空間(フーリエ変換)では
\begin{eqnarray*}
  \mathbf{G}^2\phi(G) &=& 4\pi\rho(\mathbf{G})\\
  \phi(G) &=& \frac{4\pi\rho(\mathbf{G})}{\mathbf{G}^2}
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \rho_{scr}(\mathbf{G}) &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}(2\gamma)^3}\int\exp\left(-\frac{(\mathbf{r} - \tau)^2}{4\gamma^2}\right)\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}\mathbf{r}\right)d\mathbf{r}\right]\\
  &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}}\int\exp\left(-(\mathbf{r} - \frac{\tau}{2\gamma})^2\right)\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}2\gamma\mathbf{r}\right)d\mathbf{r}\right]\\
  &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}}\int\exp\left(-\mathbf{r}^2\right)\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}2\gamma(\mathbf{r}+\frac{\tau}{2\gamma})\right)d\mathbf{r}\right]\\
  &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}}\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}\tau\right)\int\exp\left(-\mathbf{r}^2\right)\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}2\gamma\mathbf{r}\right)d\mathbf{r}\right]\\
  &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}\frac{Z_\tau}{(\pi)^{3/2}}\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}\tau\right)\int\exp\left(-(\mathbf{r}+i\mathbf{g}\gamma)^2-\gamma^2\mathbf{g}^2\right)d\mathbf{r}\right]\\
  &=& \frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\mathbf{\tau}Z_\tau\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}\tau\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{g}^2\right)\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}

静電ポテンシャル(遮蔽電荷分布)

\begin{equation}
  \phi_{scr}(\mathbf{G}) = \frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\tau Z_\tau\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}\tau\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{g}^2\right)\right]
\end{equation}
\begin{eqnarray*}
  \phi_{scr}(\mathbf{r}) &=& \frac{1}{(2\pi)^3}\int d\mathbf{r}\exp(i\mathbf{r}\mathbf{g})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}\frac{(2\pi)^3}{\Omega}Comb(\mathbf{g};\mathbf{G})\left[\sum_\tau Z_\tau\exp\left(-i\mathbf{g}\tau\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{g}^2\right)\right]\\
  &=& \sum_{\mathbf{G}}\exp(i\mathbf{r}\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}\sum_\tau Z_\tau\exp\left(-i\mathbf{G}\tau\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  &=& \sum_{\mathbf{G},\tau}\frac{4\pi Z_\tau}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}\exp\left(i\mathbf{G}(\mathbf{r}-\tau)\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)
\end{eqnarray*}

エネルギー(遮蔽電荷分布と点電荷); 同一位置どうしの相互作用込み
\begin{eqnarray*}
  E_{recp} &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau'}Z_\tau'\sum_{\mathbf{G},\tau}\frac{4\pi Z_\tau}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}\exp\left(i\mathbf{G}(\tau'-\tau)\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\tau,\tau'}\frac{4\pi Z_\tau Z_\tau'}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}\exp\left(i\mathbf{G}(\tau'-\tau)\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}\left(\sum_{\tau'}Z_{\tau'}\exp\left(i\mathbf{G}\tau'\right)\right)\left(\sum_{\tau}Z_\tau\exp\left(-i\mathbf{G}\tau\right)\right)\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}|\rho_{ion}(\mathbf{G})|^2\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}|\rho_{ion}(\mathbf{G})|^2\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  & & + \frac{1}{2}\lim_{G\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega G^2}|\rho_{ion}(0)|^2 - \frac{1}{2}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega}|\rho_{ion}(0)|^2\gamma^2\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}|\rho_{ion}(\mathbf{G})|^2\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  & & + \frac{1}{2}\lim_{G\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega G^2}\left(\sum_\tau Z_\tau\right)^2 - \frac{1}{2}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\left(\sum_\tau Z_\tau\right)^2\gamma^2
\end{eqnarray*}

エネルギー(遮蔽電荷分布と点電荷); 同一位置どうしの相互作用

遮蔽電荷分布(一個だけ)
\begin{equation}
  \rho_{scr}^{1}(\mathbf{r}) = \frac{Z}{(\pi)^{3/2}(2\gamma)^3}\exp\left(-\frac{\mathbf{r}^2}{4\gamma^2}\right)\\
\end{equation}

ガウスの法則から
\begin{eqnarray*}
  4\pi E_{scr}^1(r) r^2 &=& 4\pi \int_0^r dr' 4\pi r'^2\rho_{scr}^1(r')\\
  E_{scr}^1(r) &=& \frac{1}{r^2} \int_0^r dr' 4\pi r'^2\frac{Z}{(\pi)^{3/2}(2\gamma)^3}\exp\left(-\frac{(r')^2}{4\gamma^2}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{Z}{r^2} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)} dr' 4\pi r'^2\frac{1}{(\pi)^{3/2}}\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)\\
  &=& \frac{Z}{r^2}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)} dr' r'^2\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)
\end{eqnarray*}

静電ポテンシャルは
\begin{eqnarray*}
  \phi_{scr}^1(\infty) - \phi_{scr}^1(r) &=& - \int_r^{\infty}dr' E(r')\\
  - \phi_{scr}^1(r) &=& - \int_r^{\infty}dr' E(r')\\
  \phi_{scr}^1(r) &=& \int_r^{\infty}dr' E(r')\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 \phi_{scr}^1(r) &=& \int_r^{\infty}dr' E(r')\\
 &=& \int_r^{\infty}dr'\frac{Z}{r'^2}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r'/(2\gamma)} dr'' r''^2\exp\left(-(r'')^2\right)\\
 &=& \left[-\frac{Z}{r'}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r'/(2\gamma)} dr'' r''^2\exp\left(-(r'')^2\right)\right]_r^{\infty} - \int_r^{\infty}dr'-\frac{Z}{r'}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}}\frac{1}{2\gamma}(r'/(2\gamma))^2\exp\left(-(r'/(2\gamma))^2\right)\\
 &=& \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)} dr'' r''^2\exp\left(-(r'')^2\right)\\
 & & + \frac{1}{2\gamma}\int_{r/(2\gamma)}^{\infty}d(r'/(2\gamma))\frac{Z}{r'/(2\gamma)}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} (r'/(2\gamma))^2\exp\left(-(r'/(2\gamma))^2\right)\\
 &=& \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)} dr'' \frac{1}{2}r' 2r'\exp\left(-(r'')^2\right) + \frac{1}{2\gamma}\int_{r/(2\gamma)}^{\infty}dr'\frac{Z}{r'}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} (r')^2\exp\left(-r'^2\right)\\
 &=& - \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)} dr' \frac{1}{2}r' \frac{d}{dr'}\left(\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)\right) + \frac{1}{2\gamma}\int_{r/(2\gamma)}^{\infty}dr'Z\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} r'\exp\left(-r'^2\right)\\
 &=& - \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \left[ \frac{1}{2}r'\exp\left(-(r')^2\right) \right]_0^{r/(2\gamma)} + \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)}\frac{1}{2}\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)\\
 & & + \frac{1}{2\gamma}\frac{1}{2}\int_{r^2/(4\gamma^2)}^{\infty}dt Z\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \exp\left(-t\right)\\
 &=& - \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \frac{1}{2}\frac{r}{2\gamma}\exp\left(-\left(\frac{r}{2\gamma}\right)^2\right) + \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)}\frac{1}{2}\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)\\
 & & - \frac{1}{2\gamma}\frac{1}{2}\left[Z\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \exp\left(-t\right)\right]_{r^2/(4\gamma^2)}^{\infty}\\
 &=& - Z\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \frac{1}{4\gamma}\exp\left(-\left(\frac{r}{2\gamma}\right)^2\right) + \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)}\frac{1}{2}\exp\left(-(r')^2\right) + \frac{1}{2\gamma}\frac{1}{2}Z\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \exp\left(-r^2/(4\gamma^2)\right)\\
 &=& \frac{Z}{r}\frac{4\pi}{(\pi)^{3/2}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)}\frac{1}{2}\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)\\
 &=& \frac{Z}{r}\frac{2}{\sqrt{\pi}} \int_0^{r/(2\gamma)}\exp\left(-(r')^2\right)\\
 &=& \frac{Z}{r}\mathrm{erf}\left(r/(2\gamma)\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

$r \rightarrow 0$では

\begin{equation}
  \phi_{scr}^1(0) = \frac{2Z}{\sqrt{\pi}}\frac{1}{2\gamma} = \frac{Z}{\gamma\sqrt{\pi}}
\end{equation}

したがって、エネルギー(遮蔽電荷分布と点電荷); 同一位置どうしの相互作用は
\begin{equation}
  E_{cor} = \sum_\tau \frac{1}{2}\frac{Z_\tau}{\gamma\sqrt{\pi}}Z_\tau = \frac{1}{2}\sum_\tau \frac{Z_\tau^2}{\gamma\sqrt{\pi}}
\end{equation}

一方、点電荷と遮蔽電荷分布の重ね合わせが作るポテンシャルは
\begin{equation}
  \frac{Z}{r} - \phi_{scr}^1(r) = \frac{Z}{r}\left(1-\mathrm{erf}\left(\frac{r}{2\gamma}\right)\right) = \frac{Z}{r}\mathrm{erfc}\left(\frac{r}{2\gamma}\right)
\end{equation}

この重ね合わせと点電荷の間の相互作用エネルギーは
\begin{equation}
  E_{real} = \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\tau',\mathbf{R}; \tau \ne \tau'+\mathbf{R}}\frac{Z_\tau Z_{\tau'}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}{\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}}
\end{equation}

全部合わせて
\begin{eqnarray*}
  E_{ewald} &=& E_{real}+E_{recp}-E_{cor}\\
  &=& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau \ne \tau'+\mathbf{R}}\frac{Z_\tau Z_{\tau'}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}{\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}} \\
  & & + \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega\mathbf{G}^2}|\rho_{ion}(\mathbf{G})|^2\exp\left(-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2\right)\\
  & & + \frac{1}{2}\lim_{G\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega G^2}\left(\sum_\tau Z_\tau\right)^2 - \frac{1}{2}\frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\left(\sum_\tau Z_\tau\right)^2\gamma^2\\
  & & - \frac{1}{2}\sum_\tau \frac{Z_\tau^2}{\gamma\sqrt{\pi}}
\end{eqnarray*}


\subsection{Exchange-Correlation Energy}

\begin{equation}
E_{xc} = \int_V d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+},|\nabla \rho_{+}|,\rho_{-},|\nabla \rho_{-}|)
\end{equation}

\newpage
\section{Hellmann-Feynman Theorem}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\partial E}{\partial \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}}& = & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\right]\\
\frac{d E}{d \lambda} &=& \frac{\partial E}{\partial \lambda} + \sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\frac{\partial E}{\partial \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}}\frac{\partial \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}}{\partial \lambda} + \frac{\partial E}{\partial \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}}\frac{\partial \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}}{\partial \lambda}\right]\\
1 &=&\sum_\mathbf{G}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
0 &=&\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left[\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\right]\frac{\partial \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial \lambda}\\
 && + \sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left[\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\right]\frac{\partial \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial \lambda}\\
 && + \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\frac{\partial\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right)}{\partial \lambda}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\frac{d E}{d \lambda} &=& \frac{\partial E}{\partial \lambda} \\
&+& \sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n,\mathbf{G}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\right]\frac{\partial \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial \lambda}\\
&+& \sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n,\mathbf{G}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\right]\frac{\partial \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial \lambda}\\
&=&\frac{\partial E}{\partial \lambda} - \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\frac{\partial\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right)}{\partial \lambda}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\newpage
\section{Uniform scaling}
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathbf{r} &\rightarrow& \frac{1}{s}\mathbf{r}\\
\mathbf{G} &\rightarrow& s\mathbf{G}\\
\mathbf{k} &\rightarrow& s\mathbf{k}\\
\Omega &\rightarrow& s^{-3}\Omega_0\\
\frac{\partial f}{\partial\Omega} &=& \frac{\partial f}{\partial s}\frac{d s}{d\Omega}\\
 &=& \frac{\partial f}{\partial s}\frac{-s^4}{3\Omega_0}\\
 &=& \frac{\partial f}{\partial s}\frac{-ss^3}{3\Omega_0}\\
 &=& -s\frac{\partial f}{\partial s}\frac{1}{3\Omega}\\
s\frac{df(s\mathbf{G})}{ds} &=& s\frac{df(s\mathbf{G})}{d(s\mathbf{G})}\frac{d(s\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
 &=& \left.\frac{df}{d\mathbf{G}}\right|_{s\mathbf{G}}s\mathbf{G}\\
s\frac{d\Omega}{ds} &=& -3\Omega\\
s\frac{d\Omega^{-1}}{ds} &=& -\Omega^{-2}\times -3\Omega\\
&=& 3\Omega^{-1}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Charge}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x}) &=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\right]^\ast\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{x}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
s\frac{d\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x})}{ds} &=& 3\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x})
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsubsection{band charge}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G}) & = & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}+\mathbf{G'})\\
s\frac{\partial\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s} & = & 0
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsubsection{core charge}
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})\\
&\rightarrow&\frac{s^3}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(s(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'}))Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(s\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(s(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''}))\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
s\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s}&=&3\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})s\frac{dQ_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Kinetic Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{kinet}}{ds} &=& 2E_{kinet}
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Kinetic Energy: Bernasconi-Tosatti-Parrinello method}

REF: M. Bernasconi et al., J. Phys. Chem. Solids \textbf{36} 501-505 (1995).

\begin{eqnarray}
  E_{kinet} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\\
  &\rightarrow& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{2}\left[(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2+A_{BTP}\left(1+\mathrm{erf}\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)\right)\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{eqnarray}

\begin{eqnarray}
  &&s\frac{d}{ds}\left\{s^2(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2+A_{BTP}\left(1+\mathrm{erf}\left(\frac{s^2(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)\right)\right\}\\
  &=&2s^2(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2+A_{BTP}\frac{s^2(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2}{\sigma_{BTP}}\frac{2}{\sqrt\pi}\exp\left\{-\left(\frac{s^2(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)^2\right\}
\end{eqnarray}


\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{kinet}}{ds} &=& 2E_{kinet}\\
 & + & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})A_{BTP}\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2}{\sigma_{BTP}\sqrt\pi}\exp\left\{-\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)^2\right\}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Local potential Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{local} &=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\\
s\frac{dE_{local}}{ds} &=& 3E_{local} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\\
&=& 3E_{local} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\\
&=& 3E_{local} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{3}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau'}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{-G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau'}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{dQ_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau'}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{-G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Hartree Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{hartree} &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
s\frac{dE_{hartree}}{ds} &=& 3E_{hartree} -2E_{hartree} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}s\frac{d\rho(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
s\frac{dE_{hartree}}{ds} &=& E_{hartree} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}s\frac{d\rho(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
s\frac{dE_{hartree}}{ds} &=& E_{hartree} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Non-local potential Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{nonlocal}&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
s\frac{dE_{nonlocal}}{ds}&=&3E_{nonlocal} + \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Ewald Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{ewald} &=& \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{1}{2}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}}\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{R'}}\frac{Z_\tau Z_{\tau'}}{|\tau+\mathbf{R}-\tau'-\mathbf{R'}|}e^{-\alpha|\tau+\mathbf{R}-\tau'-\mathbf{R'}|}\\
s\frac{dE_{ewald}}{ds} &=& E_{ewald}
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Exchange-Correlation Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{xc} &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+},|\nabla \rho_{+}|,\rho_{-},|\nabla \rho_{-}|)\\
 &\rightarrow& \int_{s^{-3}V} d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+}(s),|\nabla \rho_{+}(s)|,\rho_{-}(s),|\nabla \rho_{-}(s)|)\\
 &=& s^{-3}\int_{V} d(s\mathbf{r}) f_{xc}(\rho_{+}(s\mathbf{r}/s,s),|\nabla \rho_{+}(s\mathbf{r}/s,s)|,\rho_{-}(s\mathbf{r}/s,s),|\nabla \rho_{-}(s\mathbf{r}/s,s)|)\\
 &=& s^{-3}\int_{V} d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+}(\mathbf{r}/s,s),|\nabla \rho_{+}(\mathbf{r}/s,s)|,\rho_{-}(\mathbf{r}/s,s),|\nabla \rho_{-}(\mathbf{r}/s,s)|)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{xc}}{ds} &=& -3E_{xc} + \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_{+}}s\frac{d\rho_{+}}{ds} + \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_{+}|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_{+}|}{d\nabla\rho_{+}}s\frac{d\nabla\rho_{+}}{ds}\\
&+& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc,-}}{\delta \rho_{-}}s\frac{d\rho_{-}}{ds} + \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_{-}|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_{-}|}{d\nabla\rho_{-}}s\frac{d\nabla\rho_{-}}{ds}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{d\rho}{ds} &=& s\frac{d}{ds}\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& \frac{3}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
&=& 3\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{d\nabla\rho}{ds} &=& s\frac{d}{ds}\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& \frac{3}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
&=& 4\nabla\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}s\frac{d\rho}{ds} &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\left(3\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& 3\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
&=& 3\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds} + s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}s\frac{d\nabla\rho}{ds}\\
 &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\left(4\nabla\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& -4\int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)\rho(\mathbf{r})\\
&-&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}-\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
&=& -4\int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)\rho(\mathbf{r})\\
&-&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\left(\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)\right)(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}-\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\left(\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)\right)(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
&=& -4\int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)\rho(\mathbf{r})\\
&-&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\left(\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)\right)(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}+s\frac{d\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{xc}}{ds} &=& -3E_{xc}+\sum_{\sigma}\\
& & \left[ 3\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds} + \frac{1}{2}s\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right) \right.\\
&-& 4\int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\\
&-& \left. \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\left(\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\right)(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}+\frac{1}{2}s\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right) \right]\\
&=& -3E_{xc}+3\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma - 4\sum_\sigma \int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) \\
&+& \sum_{\sigma}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}} \left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma} - \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\right)(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds} + s\frac{1}{2}\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right)\\
&=& -3E_{xc}+3\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma - 4\sum_\sigma \int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) \\
&+& \sum_{\sigma}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds} + s\frac{1}{2}\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Hellmann-Feynman}
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&- \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right)}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
