&=&-\frac{3}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&-&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&-& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Total Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{total}}{ds} &=& 2E_{kinet} + 3E_{local} + E_{hartree} + 3 E_{nonlocal} + E_{ewald} - 3E_{xc}\\
 &+& 3\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma - 4\sum_\sigma \int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma \\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}s\frac{d\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \sum_{\sigma}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}} V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\left(s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds} + s\frac{1}{2}\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\right)\\
&-&\frac{3}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&-&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&-& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=& 2E_{kinet} + 3E_{local} + E_{hartree} + 3 E_{nonlocal} + E_{ewald} - 3E_{xc}\\
&+& 3\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma - 4\sum_\sigma \int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma \\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}\left(\sum_\tau V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G}) + \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2} + V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\right)s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}\left(D_{p,q}^{\tau}-\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right)\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\left(D_{p,q}^{\tau}-\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right)\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \sum_{\sigma}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}} V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{1}{2}\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
&-&\frac{3}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
V_{ionic}(\mathbf{G}) := \sum_\tau V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
V_{hartree}(\mathbf{G}) := \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) := \sum_\tau V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G}) + \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2} + V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 && \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}\left(\sum_\tau V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G}) + \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2} + V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\right)s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{d\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{-G})}{ds}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\\
 & & \times\left(3\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\right.\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})s\frac{dQ_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\left.\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\right)\\
 &=& \frac{3}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{dQ_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
D_{p,q;\sigma}^{\tau;scr} := D_{p,q}^{\tau} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{total}}{ds} &=& 2E_{kinet} + 3E_{local} + E_{hartree} + 3 E_{nonlocal} + E_{ewald} - 3E_{xc}\\
 &+& 3\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma - 4\sum_\sigma \int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma \\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}\left(D_{p,q;\sigma}^{\tau;scr}-\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right)\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\left(D_{p,q;\sigma}^{\tau;scr}-\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right)\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{dQ_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
 &+& \sum_{\sigma}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}} V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{1}{2}\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
 &+& \frac{3}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\\
&-&\frac{3}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} := \langle\beta_{\mathbf{k},\tau,p}|\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\rangle = \sum_{\mathbf{G}}\beta_{\tau,p}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^\mathbf{k} := \langle s\frac{d\beta_{\mathbf{k},\tau,p}}{ds}|\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\rangle = \sum_{\mathbf{G}}s\frac{d\beta_{\tau,p}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{ds}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
s\frac{dE_{total}}{ds} &=& 2E_{kinet} + 3E_{local} + E_{hartree} + 3 E_{nonlocal} + E_{ewald} - 3E_{xc}\\
 &+& 3\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma - 4\sum_\sigma \int_V d\mathbf{r} \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\rho_\sigma \\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}s\frac{dV^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{ds}\rho(\mathbf{-G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n,\tau,p,q}\Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left(D_{p,q;\sigma}^{\tau;scr}-\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right)P_{\tau,q;,\sigma,n}^\mathbf{k}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n,\tau,p,q,}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left(D_{p,q;\sigma}^{\tau;scr}-\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right)\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^\mathbf{k}\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n,\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;,\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{dQ_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^\mathbf{k}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}} V_{xc,\sigma}(\mathbf{G})s\frac{1}{2}\frac{d\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{ds}\\
 &+& \frac{3}{\Omega}\sum_{\sigma,\mathbf{G}}V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\\
&-&\frac{3}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} Q_{p,q}^{\tau}P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^\mathbf{k}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\section{Local potential: short range and long range}

\begin{equation}
  V(r) = V_{short}(r) - \frac{Z}{r}\left(a_1\mathrm{erf}(\sqrt{a_2}r) + a_3\mathrm{erf}(\sqrt{a_4}r)\right),
\end{equation}
ここで、
\begin{equation}
  a_1 + a_3 = 1 
\end{equation}

\subsection{$g > 0$}

\begin{equation}
  V(g) = V_{short}(g) - \frac{4\pi Z}{g^2}\left(a_1\exp(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}) + a_3\exp(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4})\right)
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray}
  g\frac{dV(g)}{dg} &=& g\frac{dV_{short}(g)}{dg} - g(-2)\frac{4\pi Z}{g^3}\left(a_1\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}\right) + a_3\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4}\right)\right)\\
  &-& g\frac{4\pi Z}{g^2}\left(-\frac{2g}{4a_2}a_1\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}\right) -\frac{2g}{4a_4}a_3\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4}\right)\right)\\
  &=& g\frac{dV_{short}(g)}{dg} + 2\frac{4\pi Z}{g^2}\left(a_1\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}\right) + a_3\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4}\right)\right)\\
  &+& \frac{1}{2}\frac{4\pi Z}{g^2}\left(\frac{g^2}{a_2}a_1\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}\right) +\frac{g^2}{a_4}a_3\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4}\right)\right)\\
  &=& g\frac{dV_{short}(g)}{dg} + 2\frac{4\pi Z}{g^2}\left(a_1\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}\right) + a_3\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4}\right)\right)\\
  &+& \frac{1}{2}4\pi Z\left(\frac{a_1}{a_2}\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_2}\right) +\frac{a_3}{a_4}\exp\left(-\frac{g^2}{4a_4}\right)\right)
\end{eqnarray}

\subsection{$g = 0$}

\begin{equation}
  V(0) = V_{short}(0) + \pi Z\left(\frac{a_1}{a_2}+\frac{a_3}{a_4}\right)
\end{equation}

\section{operators}

\subsection{S}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \langle \mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}|S|\psi_\mathbf{k'}\rangle\\
 &=& \int d\mathbf{r} d\mathbf{r}' \frac{1}{\sqrt{N_{cell}\Omega}}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}\Bigg(\delta(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{r}') + \sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}} \beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{r}'-\mathbf{R})\Bigg)\\
 & &\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\frac{1}{\sqrt{N_{cell}\Omega}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')e^{i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r'}}\\
 &=&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\int d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')e^{i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r'}}\\
 & &+ \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\Bigg(\int d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r}-\mathbf{R})\Bigg)Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\Bigg(\int d\mathbf{r}'\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{r}'-\mathbf{R})e^{i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r'}}\Bigg)\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')\\
 &=&\delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}'}\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')\delta_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'}\\
 & &+ \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q,\mathbf{R}}\Bigg(\int d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r})\Bigg)e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{R}}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\Bigg(\int d\mathbf{r}'\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{r}')e^{i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r'}}\Bigg)e^{i\mathbf{k}'\cdot\mathbf{R}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')\\
 &=&\delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G})\\
 & &+ \frac{\delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}'}}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\Bigg(\int d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{r})\Bigg)Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\Bigg(\int d\mathbf{r}'\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{r}')e^{i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r'}}\Bigg)\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')\\
 &=&\delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{\delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}'}}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}')\phi_{\mathbf{k}'}(\mathbf{G}')
\end{eqnarray*}


\section{partial density of states}

expectation of $|p\rangle\langle p|$

\begin{eqnarray*}
& & \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast\int d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}p(\mathbf{r})p(\mathbf{r}')^{\ast}e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast\int d\mathbf{r}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}}p(\mathbf{r}) \int d\mathbf{r}'p(\mathbf{r}')^{\ast}e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast p(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}) p(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')^{\ast}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast p(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}p(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')^{\ast}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\Bigg|\sum_{\mathbf{G}'}p(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')^{\ast}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\Bigg|^2\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\section{partial density of states by a Wannier function}

reciprocal space representation of a Wannier function is
\[
 w_j(\mathbf{r}) = \frac{1}{N_{cell}\sqrt{\Omega}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{G}} w_{\mathbf{k},j}(\mathbf{G})\exp[i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}],
\]
where
\[
 \sum_\mathbf{G} w_{\mathbf{k},j}(\mathbf{G})^\ast w_{\mathbf{k},j}(\mathbf{G}) = 1.
\]

expectation of $|p\rangle\langle p|$ is

\begin{eqnarray*}
& & \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast\int d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}} \\
& & \frac{1}{N_{cell}\sqrt{\Omega}}\sum_{\mathbf{k}',\mathbf{G}''} w_{\mathbf{k}',j}(\mathbf{G}'')\exp[i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}'')\cdot\mathbf{r}]
\frac{1}{N_{cell}\sqrt{\Omega}}\sum_{\mathbf{k}'',\mathbf{G}'''} w_{\mathbf{k}',j}(\mathbf{G}''')^\ast\exp[-i(\mathbf{k}''+\mathbf{G}''')\cdot\mathbf{r}'] \\
& & e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}^3\Omega^2}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}',\mathbf{k}''}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}',\mathbf{G}'',\mathbf{G}'''}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast\int d\mathbf{r}d\mathbf{r'}e^{-i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\cdot\mathbf{r}} \\
& & w_{\mathbf{k}',j}(\mathbf{G}'')\exp[i(\mathbf{k}'+\mathbf{G}'')\cdot\mathbf{r}]
 w_{\mathbf{k}',j}(\mathbf{G}''')^\ast\exp[-i(\mathbf{k}''+\mathbf{G}''')\cdot\mathbf{r}'] \\
& & e^{i(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G}')\cdot\mathbf{r}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}^3\Omega^2}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}',\mathbf{k}''}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}',\mathbf{G}'',\mathbf{G}'''}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast 
w_{\mathbf{k}',j}(\mathbf{G}'') w_{\mathbf{k}',j}(\mathbf{G}''')^\ast
\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
& & \delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}'}\delta_{\mathbf{k},\mathbf{k}''}
\delta_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}''}\delta_{\mathbf{G}',\mathbf{G}'''} N_{cell}^2\Omega^2\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'}\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})^\ast 
w_{\mathbf{k},j}(\mathbf{G}) w_{\mathbf{k},j}(\mathbf{G}')^\ast
\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G}')\\
&=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k}}\left|\sum_{\mathbf{G}}w_{\mathbf{k},j}(\mathbf{G})^\ast\phi_{\mathbf{k}}(\mathbf{G})\right|^2\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\section{Force}
\subsection{Ewald Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{dE_{ewald}}{d\tau} &=& \frac{d}{d\tau}\Bigg[\frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_1,\tau_2,\mathbf{R} (\tau_1\ne\tau_2)}Z_{\tau_1}Z_{\tau_2}\frac{1}{|\tau_1-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau_1-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\Bigg] \\
&=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}S^Z(\mathbf{G})\frac{d}{d\tau}\sum_{\tau_2}Z_{\tau_2}e^{i\tau_2\cdot\mathbf{G}}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\frac{d}{d\tau}\sum_{\tau_1}Z_{\tau_1}e^{-i\tau_1\cdot\mathbf{G}}S^Z(\mathbf{G})^\ast\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_2,\mathbf{R} (\tau_2\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau_2}\bigg(-\frac{\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|^3}\bigg)\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_1,\mathbf{R} (\tau_1\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau_1}Z_{\tau}\frac{\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}|^3}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_2,\mathbf{R} (\tau_2\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau_2}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}\bigg(\frac{\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}}{2\gamma|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}\bigg)\frac{-2}{\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_1,\mathbf{R} (\tau_1\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau_1}Z_{\tau}\frac{1}{|\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}|}\bigg(-\frac{\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}}{2\gamma|\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}|}\bigg)\frac{-2}{\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau_1-\tau-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) \\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{-\mathbf{G}\ne 0} S^Z(\mathbf{G})i\mathbf{G}Z_{\tau}e^{i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}} \frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0} (-i\mathbf{G})Z_{\tau}e^{-i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}}S^Z(\mathbf{G})^\ast  \frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_2,\mathbf{R} (\tau_2\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau_2}\bigg(-\frac{\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|^3}\bigg)\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_1,-\mathbf{R} (\tau_1\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau_1}Z_{\tau}\frac{\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}}{|\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}|^3}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_2,\mathbf{R} (\tau_2\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau_2}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}\bigg(\frac{\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}}{2\gamma|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|}\bigg)\frac{-2}{\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau_2-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau_1,-\mathbf{R} (\tau_1\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau_1}Z_{\tau}\frac{1}{|\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}|}\bigg(-\frac{\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}}{2\gamma|\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}|}\bigg)\frac{-2}{\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau_1-\tau+\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) \\
 &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0} Z_{\tau}\mathbf{G}[ iS^Z(\mathbf{G}) e^{i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}} - iS^Z(\mathbf{G})^\ast e^{-i\tau\mathbf{G}}]\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & +\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{R} (\tau'\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\bigg(-\frac{\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^3}\bigg)\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & -\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\sum_{\tau',\mathbf{R} (\tau'\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) \\
 &=& \frac{-1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0} Z_{\tau}\mathbf{G} \Im[ S^Z(\mathbf{G}) e^{i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}} ] \frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} - \\
 & & \sum_{\tau',\mathbf{R} (\tau'\ne\tau)}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}\bigg[\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) + \frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\bigg] \\
 &=& \frac{-1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0} Z_{\tau}\mathbf{G} \Im[ S^Z(\mathbf{G}) e^{i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}} ] \frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} - \\
 & & \sum_{\tau'\ne\tau,\mathbf{R}}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}\bigg[\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) + \frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\bigg]
\end{eqnarray*}

\section{structure factor}
\begin{equation}
  S(\mathbf{G}) = \sum_\tau \exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau)
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
  P(\mathbf{G}) = S(\mathbf{G})^\ast S(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \sum_{\mathbf{G}}P(\mathbf{G}) & = & \sum_{\mathbf{G}}S(\mathbf{G})^\ast S(\mathbf{G})\\
  & = & \sum_{\mathbf{G}}\sum_{\tau'} \exp(i\mathbf{G}\tau')\sum_\tau \exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau) \\
  & = & \sum_{\mathbf{G},\tau',\tau}\exp[i\mathbf{G}(\tau'-\tau)] \\
  & = & \sum_{\tau',\tau}\delta_{\tau,\tau'}N_{cell} \\
  & = & N_{atom}N_{cell} \\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
  \frac{dS(\mathbf{G})}{d\tau} = -i\mathbf{G}\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau)
\end{equation}

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \frac{dP(\mathbf{G})}{d\tau} & = & S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\frac{dS(\mathbf{G})}{d\tau} + S(\mathbf{G})\frac{dS(\mathbf{G})^\ast}{d\tau}\\
  & = & -i\mathbf{G} S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau) + i\mathbf{G}S(\mathbf{G})\exp(i\mathbf{G}\tau)\\
  & = & -i\mathbf{G} [ S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau) - S(\mathbf{G})\exp(i\mathbf{G}\tau) ] \\
  & = & -i\mathbf{G} [ S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau) - (S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau))^\ast ] \\
  & = & -i\mathbf{G} [ 2i \Im(S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau)) ] \\
  & = & 2\mathbf{G} \Im[S(\mathbf{G})^\ast\exp(-i\mathbf{G}\tau)] \\
  & = & 2\mathbf{G} [\Re (S(\mathbf{G})^\ast)\sin(-\mathbf{G}\tau) + \Im (S(\mathbf{G})^\ast)\cos(-\mathbf{G}\tau) ] \\
  & = & 2\mathbf{G} [ - \Re (S(\mathbf{G}))\sin(\mathbf{G}\tau) - \Im (S(\mathbf{G}))\cos(\mathbf{G}\tau) ] \\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{equation}
  \frac{dP(\mathbf{G})^{m}}{d\tau} = m P(\mathbf{G})^{m-1}\frac{dP(\mathbf{G})}{d\tau}
\end{equation}

\newpage

\section{Non-uniform scaling}
\begin{eqnarray*}
s_{xy} &=& s_{yx}\\
s_{yz} &=& s_{zy}\\
s_{zx} &=& s_{xz}\\
s_{1} &=& s_{xx}\\
s_{2} &=& s_{yy}\\
s_{3} &=& s_{zz}\\
s_{4} &=& s_{yz}\\
s_{5} &=& s_{zx}\\
s_{6} &=& s_{xy}\\
\mathbf{G} &\rightarrow& (1+s)\mathbf{G}\\
\frac{\partial f(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_{\nu}} &=& \frac{\partial f}{\partial G_{i}}\frac{\partial G_{i}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\\
G_x &=& G_x^0 +s_{xx}G_x^0 + s_{xy}G_y^0 + s_{xz}G_z^0\\
G_y &=& G_y^0 +s_{yx}G_x^0 + s_{yy}G_y^0 + s_{yz}G_z^0\\
G_z &=& G_z^0 +s_{zx}G_x^0 + s_{zy}G_y^0 + s_{zz}G_z^0\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\[
\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
\frac{\partial G_x}{\partial s_1} & \frac{\partial G_y}{\partial s_1} & \frac{\partial G_z}{\partial s_1} \\
\frac{\partial G_x}{\partial s_2} & \frac{\partial G_y}{\partial s_2} & \frac{\partial G_z}{\partial s_2} \\
\frac{\partial G_x}{\partial s_3} & \frac{\partial G_y}{\partial s_3} & \frac{\partial G_z}{\partial s_3} \\
\frac{\partial G_x}{\partial s_4} & \frac{\partial G_y}{\partial s_4} & \frac{\partial G_z}{\partial s_4} \\
\frac{\partial G_x}{\partial s_5} & \frac{\partial G_y}{\partial s_5} & \frac{\partial G_z}{\partial s_5} \\
\frac{\partial G_x}{\partial s_6} & \frac{\partial G_y}{\partial s_6} & \frac{\partial G_z}{\partial s_6} \\
\end{array}
\right)
=
\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
 G_x^0 & 0     & 0 \\
 0     & G_y^0 & 0 \\
 0     & 0     & G_z^0 \\
 0     & G_z^0 & G_y^0 \\
 G_z^0 & 0     & G_x^0 \\
 G_y^0 & G_x^0 & 0     \\
\end{array}
\right)
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \frac{\partial f(G)}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{df(G)}{dG}\frac{\partial G}{\partial s_\nu}\\
   &=& \frac{df(G)}{dG}\frac{\partial G}{\partial G_i}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
   &=& \frac{df(G)}{dG}\frac{G_i}{G}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
   &=& G\frac{df(G)}{dG}\frac{G_i}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\[
\frac{1}{G^2}\left(
\begin{array}{c}
G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_1}\\
G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_2}\\
G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_3}\\
G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_4}\\
G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_5}\\
G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_6}\\
\end{array}
\right)
=
\frac{1}{G^2}\left(
\begin{array}{c}
 G_x^2\\
 G_y^2\\
 G_z^2\\
 2 G_y G_z\\
 2 G_z G_x\\
 2 G_x G_y\\
\end{array}
\right)
=
\left(
\begin{array}{c}
 \hat{G}_x^2\\
 \hat{G}_y^2\\
 \hat{G}_z^2\\
 2 \hat{G}_y \hat{G}_z\\
 2 \hat{G}_z \hat{G}_x\\
 2 \hat{G}_x \hat{G}_y\\
\end{array}
\right)
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\frac{\partial \hat{G}_i}{\partial G_j}\frac{\partial G_j}{\partial s_\nu}\\
  \frac{\partial \hat{G}_i}{\partial G_j} &=& \frac{\partial (G_i/G)}{\partial G_j}\\
  &=& \frac{\delta_{i,j}}{G} - G_i \frac{G_j}{G^3}\\
  \frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\left(\frac{\delta_{i,j}}{G} - G_i \frac{G_j}{G^3}\right)\frac{\partial G_j}{\partial s_\nu}\\
  &=& \frac{1}{G}\frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\left(\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} - G_i \frac{G_j}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_j}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{G}\frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} - \frac{1}{G}\left(G_i\frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\right)\left(\frac{G_j}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_j}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\\
  &=& \frac{1}{G}\frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} - \left(\hat{G}_i\frac{\partial f(\hat{G})}{\partial \hat{G}_i}\right)\left(\frac{G_j}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_j}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \Omega & = & \det(\mathbf{a}_1,\mathbf{a}_2,\mathbf{a}_3)\\
  \mathbf{a}_i & \rightarrow & ((1+s)^t)^{-1}\mathbf{a}_i = (1+s)^{-1}\mathbf{a}_i = (1 - s + O(s^2))\mathbf{a}_i\\
  \Omega &\rightarrow& \det{[((1+s)^t)^{-1}]}\Omega = \frac{\Omega}{\det{(1+s)}}\\
  \frac{1}{\Omega} &\rightarrow& \frac{\det{(1+s)}}{\Omega}\\
  \det{(1+s)} & = & 1 + s_1 + s_2 + s_3 + O(s^2)\\
  \left.\frac{\partial\det{(1+s)}}{\partial s_\nu}\right|_{s = 0} & = & 1;\quad \nu = 1,2,3\\
  \left.\frac{\partial\det{(1+s)}}{\partial s_\nu}\right|_{s = 0} & = & 0;\quad \nu = 4,5,6\\
  \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu} & = & \Omega^{-1};\quad \nu = 1,2,3\\
  \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu} & = & 0;\quad \nu = 4,5,6\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
  \mathbf{r} &\rightarrow& ((1+s)^t)^{-1}\mathbf{r} = (1+s)^{-1}\mathbf{r} = (1-s)\mathbf{r} + O(s^2)\\
  \frac{\partial f(\mathbf{r})}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial f}{\partial r_i}\frac{\partial r_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
  r_x &=& r_x^0 - s_{xx} r_x^0 - s_{xy} r_y^0 - s_{xz} r_z^0 + O(s^2)\\
  r_y &=& r_y^0 - s_{yx} r_x^0 - s_{yy} r_y^0 - s_{yz} r_z^0 + O(s^2)\\
  r_z &=& r_z^0 - s_{zx} r_x^0 - s_{zy} r_y^0 - s_{zz} r_z^0 + O(s^2)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\[
\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
\frac{\partial r_x}{\partial s_1} & \frac{\partial r_y}{\partial s_1} & \frac{\partial r_z}{\partial s_1} \\
\frac{\partial r_x}{\partial s_2} & \frac{\partial r_y}{\partial s_2} & \frac{\partial r_z}{\partial s_2} \\
\frac{\partial r_x}{\partial s_3} & \frac{\partial r_y}{\partial s_3} & \frac{\partial r_z}{\partial s_3} \\
\frac{\partial r_x}{\partial s_4} & \frac{\partial r_y}{\partial s_4} & \frac{\partial r_z}{\partial s_4} \\
\frac{\partial r_x}{\partial s_5} & \frac{\partial r_y}{\partial s_5} & \frac{\partial r_z}{\partial s_5} \\
\frac{\partial r_x}{\partial s_6} & \frac{\partial r_y}{\partial s_6} & \frac{\partial r_z}{\partial s_6} \\
\end{array}
\right)_{s=0}
=
-\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
 r_x^0 & 0     & 0 \\
 0     & r_y^0 & 0 \\
 0     & 0     & r_z^0 \\
 0     & r_z^0 & r_y^0 \\
 r_z^0 & 0     & r_x^0 \\
 r_y^0 & r_x^0 & 0     \\
\end{array}
\right)
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
\left(\begin{array}{c}
  \varepsilon_{xx}\\
  \varepsilon_{yx}\\
  \varepsilon_{zx}\\
\end{array}\right)
&=&
\left(\begin{array}{c}
  \frac{\partial[(1-s_{xx})x-s_{xy}y-s_{xz}z]}{\partial x}\\
  \frac{1}{2}(\frac{\partial[(1-s_{xx})x-s_{xy}y-s_{xz}z]}{\partial y} + \frac{\partial[-s_{yx}x + (1-s_{yy})y-s_{zy}z]}{\partial x})\\
  \frac{1}{2}(\frac{\partial[(1-s_{xx})x-s_{xy}y-s_{xz}z]}{\partial z} + \frac{\partial[-s_{zx}x - s_{zy}y  + (1-s_{zz})z]}{\partial x})\\
\end{array}\right) + O(s^2)\\
&=&
\left(\begin{array}{c}
 -s_{xx}\\
  \frac{-s_{xy} -s_{yx}}{2}\\
  \frac{-s_{xz} -s_{zx}}{2}\\
\end{array}\right) + O(s^2)\\
&=&
\left(\begin{array}{c}
 -s_{xx}\\
 -s_{yx}\\
 -s_{zx}\\
\end{array}\right) + O(s^2)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\[
\left(\begin{array}{ccc}
  \varepsilon_{xx} & \varepsilon_{xy} & \varepsilon_{xz}\\
  \varepsilon_{yx} & \varepsilon_{yy} & \varepsilon_{yz}\\
  \varepsilon_{zx} & \varepsilon_{zy} & \varepsilon_{zz}\\
\end{array}\right)
=
- \left(\begin{array}{ccc}
  s_{xx} & s_{xy} & s_{xz}\\
  s_{yx} & s_{yy} & s_{yz}\\
  s_{zx} & s_{zy} & s_{zz}\\
\end{array}\right) + O(s^2)
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \frac{\partial}{\partial s_\nu}\left(e^{-i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}}f(G)g(\hat{G})\right)\\
 &=& e^{-i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\partial f(G)}{\partial s_\nu}g(\hat{G}) + f(G)\frac{\partial g(\hat{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\\
 &=& e^{-i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}}\left(G\frac{df(G)}{dG}\frac{G_i}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}g(\hat{G}) + f(G)\frac{1}{G}\frac{\partial g(\hat{G})}{\partial\hat{G}_i}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} - f(G)\left(\hat{G}_i\frac{\partial g(\hat{G})}{\partial\hat{G}_i}\right)\left(\frac{G_j}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_j}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\right)\\
 &=& e^{-i\tau\cdot\mathbf{G}}\left[\left(G\frac{df(G)}{dG}g(\hat{G}) - f(G)\left(\hat{G}_i\frac{\partial g(\hat{G})}{\partial\hat{G}_i}\right)\right) \frac{G_i}{G^2}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} + f(G)\frac{\partial g(\hat{G})}{\partial\hat{G}_i}\frac{1}{G}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}
\subsection{definitions}

\begin{equation}
P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} := \langle\beta_{\mathbf{k},\tau,p}|\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\rangle = \sum_{\mathbf{G}}\beta_{\tau,p}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^\mathbf{k} := \langle \frac{\partial\beta_{\mathbf{k},\tau,p}}{\partial s_\nu}|\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\rangle = \sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,p}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
  \hat{s} := 1+s
\end{equation}

\subsection{Exchange-Correlation Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{xc} &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+},|\nabla \rho_{+}|,\rho_{-},|\nabla \rho_{-}|)\\
 &\rightarrow& \int_{\hat{s}^{-1}V} d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+}(s),|\nabla \rho_{+}(s)|,\rho_{-}(s),|\nabla \rho_{-}(s)|)\\
 &=& \int_{\hat{s}^{-1}V} d(\hat{s}^{-1}\hat{s}\mathbf{r}) f_{xc}(\rho_{+}(\hat{s}^{-1}\hat{s}\mathbf{r},s),|\nabla \rho_{+}(\hat{s}^{-1}\hat{s}\mathbf{r},s)|,\rho_{-}(\hat{s}^{-1}\hat{s}\mathbf{r},s),|\nabla \rho_{-}(\hat{s}^{-1}\hat{s}\mathbf{r},s)|)\\
 &=& \det{\hat{s}}^{-1}\int_{V} d\mathbf{r} f_{xc}(\rho_{+}(\hat{s}^{-1}\mathbf{r},s),|\nabla \rho_{+}(\hat{s}^{-1}\mathbf{r},s)|,\rho_{-}(\hat{s}^{-1}\mathbf{r},s),|\nabla \rho_{-}(\hat{s}^{-1}\mathbf{r},s)|)\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\partial E_{xc}}{\partial s_{\nu}} &=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_{+}}\frac{\partial\rho_{+}}{\partial s_{\nu}} + \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_{+}|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_{+}|}{d\nabla\rho_{+}}\frac{\partial\nabla\rho_{+}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\\
&+& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc,-}}{\delta \rho_{-}}\frac{\partial\rho_{-}}{\partial s_{\nu}} + \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_{-}|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_{-}|}{d\nabla\rho_{-}}\frac{\partial\nabla\rho_{-}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\partial\rho}{\partial s_{\nu}} &=& \frac{\partial}{\partial s_{\nu}}\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\sum_\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\partial\nabla\rho}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial}{\partial s_\nu}\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
&=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\left(\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + \frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
&=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\left(\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + \frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\Big(\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\Big)e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}


\[
\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + \frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}
=
\left(
\begin{array}{c}
1\\
1\\
1\\
0\\
0\\
0\\
\end{array}
\right)
\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
G_x & G_y & G_z\\
\end{array}
\right)
+
\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
 G_x & 0     & 0 \\
 0     & G_y & 0 \\
 0     & 0     & G_z \\
 0     & G_z & G_y \\
 G_z & 0     & G_x \\
 G_y & G_x & 0     \\
\end{array}
\right)
=
\left(
\begin{array}{ccc}
 2G_x & G_y  & G_z \\
 G_x  & 2G_y & G_z \\
 G_x  & G_y  & 2G_z \\
 0     & G_z & G_y \\
 G_z & 0     & G_x \\
 G_y & G_x & 0     \\
\end{array}
\right)
\]

\begin{eqnarray*}
\int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\frac{\partial\rho}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\left(\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
&=& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}\rho(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho}(\mathbf{G})\left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\\
\end{eqnarray*}


\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\frac{\partial\nabla\rho}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &=& \int_V d\mathbf{r} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\left(\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + \frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G}i\mathbf{G}\Big(\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\Big)e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{r}}\right)\\
&=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho|}{d\nabla\rho}\right)(-\mathbf{G})\left[\left(i\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho(\mathbf{G}) + i\mathbf{G}\Big(\frac{\partial \rho_{core}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{\partial\rho_{pcc}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\Big)\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\partial E_{xc}}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_\nu}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})\left[\left(i\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})
 + i\mathbf{G}\Big(\frac{\partial\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\Big)\right]\\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_\nu}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})\left(i\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &-& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\right)(-\mathbf{G})\left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_\nu}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} \left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma} -\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\right)(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})\left(i\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial \det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) \\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})\left(i\Omega\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\mathbf{G} + i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\right)\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial \det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) - \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu} \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})(-i\mathbf{G})\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial \det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) - \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu} \sum_\sigma\int_Vd\mathbf{r}\nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(\mathbf{r})\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial \det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r}\left[ \frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta \rho_\sigma} - \nabla\cdot\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)\right]_{\mathbf{r}}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
&=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial \det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Charge}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x}) &=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\left[\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})e^{i\mathbf{G}\mathbf{x}}\right]^\ast\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}e^{i\mathbf{G'}\mathbf{x}}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\frac{\partial\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x})}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{x})
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsubsection{band charge}

\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G}) & = & \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}+\mathbf{G'})\\
\frac{\partial\rho_{\phi}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} & = & 0
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsubsection{core charge}
\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\partial\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}&=&\frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{\partial s_\nu}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&+&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},n}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\mathbf{G''}}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G''})}{\partial s_\nu}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G''})\\
&=&\frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_{core;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega} \times\\
& & \sum_{\mathbf{k},n} \sum_{\tau,p,q}  \left[  \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} + P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} + P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G}) \Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Kinetic Energy: Bernasconi-Tosatti-Parrinello method}

REF: M. Bernasconi et al., J. Phys. Chem. Solids \textbf{36} 501-505 (1995).

\begin{eqnarray*}
  E_{kinet} &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{2}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\\
  &\rightarrow& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\frac{1}{2}\left[(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2+A_{BTP}\left(1+\mathrm{erf}\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)\right)\right]\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
  &&\frac{\partial}{\partial s_\nu}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2\\
  &=&2(k_i+G_i)\frac{\partial (k_i+G_i)}{\partial s_\nu}
\end{eqnarray*}
\begin{eqnarray*}
  &&\frac{\partial}{\partial s_\nu}\left\{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2+A_{BTP}\left(1+\mathrm{erf}\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)\right)\right\}\\
  &=&2(k_i+G_i)\frac{\partial (k_i+G_i)}{\partial s_\nu}+A_{BTP}\frac{k_i+G_i}{\sigma_{BTP}}\frac{\partial (k_i+G_i)}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{2}{\sqrt\pi}\exp\left\{-\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)^2\right\}\\
  &=&2(k_i+G_i)\frac{\partial (k_i+G_i)}{\partial s_\nu}\left[1 + \frac{A_{BTP}}{\sigma_{BTP}\sqrt\pi}\exp\left\{-\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)^2\right\}\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}


\begin{eqnarray*}
 \frac{\partial E_{kinet}}{\partial s_\nu} & = &
 \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\times\\
 & & (k_i+G_i)\frac{\partial (k_i+G_i)}{\partial s_\nu}\left[1 + \frac{A_{BTP}}{\sigma_{BTP}\sqrt\pi}\exp\left\{-\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)^2\right\}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}


\subsection{Local potential Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{local} &=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\\
\frac{\partial E_{local}}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{local} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho(\mathbf{-G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
&=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{local} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{\partial s_\nu}
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Hartree Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{hartree} &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
\frac{\partial E_{hartree}}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{hartree} - \frac{1}{2\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{8\pi G_i}{(\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2)^2}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial\rho(\mathbf{-G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{hartree} - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Non-local potential Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{nonlocal}&=&\frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
\frac{\partial E_{nonlocal}}{\partial s_\nu}&=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{nonlocal} + \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})D_{p,q}^{\tau}\sum_{\mathbf{G'}}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{\partial s_\nu}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{nonlocal} + \frac{1}{N_{cell} \Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\left[ \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} D_{p,q}^{\tau} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} +  P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} D_{p,q}^{\tau}\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}} \right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}


\subsection{Hellmann-Feynman}
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&- \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\frac{\partial\left(\frac{1}{\Omega}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\right)}{\partial s_\nu}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&-\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&-&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&-& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G'}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\sum_{\tau,p,q}\beta_{\tau,p}(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\frac{\partial\beta_{\tau,q}^\ast(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G'})}{\partial s_\nu}\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G'})\\
&=&-\frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} Q_{p,q}^{\tau} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
&-&\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}\left[ \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} + P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^\mathbf{k}\right]\\
\end{eqnarray*}


\subsection{Ewald Energy}

\begin{eqnarray*}
E_{ewald} &=& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} \\
 & & + \frac{1}{2\Omega}\bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2} - \frac{1}{2\Omega}\bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2 4\pi\gamma^2 \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau\ne\tau',\mathbf{R}}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & +\frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R} (\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}^2\frac{1}{|\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma}) \\
 & & - \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}^2\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt{\pi}}\\
\frac{\partial E_{ewald}}{\partial s_\nu} &=& \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial \Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\left[\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} + \bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2} - \bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2 4\pi\gamma^2 \right] \\
 &-&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\left[\frac{1}{G^2} + \gamma^2 \right]\frac{4\pi}{G^2} e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} \\
 &-& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau'\ne\tau,\mathbf{R}}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\bigg[\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) + \frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\bigg] \times \\
 & & \frac{\tau_i-\tau'_i-\mathbf{R}_i}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}\frac{\partial (\tau_i-\tau'_i-\mathbf{R}_i)}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &-& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}(\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}^2\bigg[\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) + \frac{1}{|\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\bigg] \frac{\mathbf{R}_i}{|\mathbf{R}|^2}\frac{\partial\mathbf{R}_i}{\partial s_\nu}
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Local + Hatree + Exchange-Correlation Energy}
\begin{equation}
  \rho^a_\sigma = \rho_\sigma + \frac{1}{2}\rho_{pcc;total}
\end{equation}
\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{local} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}E_{hartree} - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial\rho_{core}(\mathbf{-G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{G})\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\\
&+& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc} + \frac{\partial \det{\hat{s}}}{\partial s_{\nu}}\sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G})i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
&+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \left(\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right) \\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\left(E_{local} + E_{hartree} + \sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\right) + \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G}) i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu} \rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} \\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} \left( \sum_\tau V^\tau(\mathbf{G}) + \lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2+\alpha^2}\rho(\mathbf{G}) + V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G}) \right) \frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} \\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\left(E_{local} + E_{hartree} + \sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r})\right) + \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G}) i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu} \rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} \\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{core; \sigma}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} \\
 &=& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\left[\frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G}) + \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\right. \times\\
 & & \left.\sum_{\mathbf{k},n} \sum_{\tau,p,q}  \left[  \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} + P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}} + P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G}) \Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\right]\right]\\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\right]\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \frac{\partial (E_{local}+E_{hartree}+E_{xc})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\left(E_{local} + E_{hartree} + \sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\right)\\
 &+& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G}) i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu} \rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})\right]\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Local + Hatree + Exchange-Correlation Energy\\ + Non-Local + Hellmann-Feynman}
\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \frac{\partial (E_{local}+E_{hartree}+E_{xc}+E_{non-local}+E_{hellmann-feynman})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\left(E_{local} + E_{non-local} + E_{hartree} + \sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\right)\\
 &+& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G}) i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu} \rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[D_{p,q}^{\tau} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G}) - \epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[D_{p,q}^{\tau} + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(-\mathbf{G}) - \epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right]\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &-& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} Q_{p,q}^{\tau} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &=& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\left(E_{local} + E_{non-local} + E_{hartree} + \sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\right)\\
 &+& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G}) i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu} \rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[D_{p,q}^{\tau;scr} - \epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[D_{p,q}^{\tau;scr} - \epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right]\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &-& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} Q_{p,q}^{\tau} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
\end{eqnarray*}

\subsection{Total Energy}
\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \frac{\partial E_{total}}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\times\\
 & & (k_i+G_i)\frac{\partial (k_i+G_i)}{\partial s_\nu}\left[1 + \frac{A_{BTP}}{\sigma_{BTP}\sqrt\pi}\exp\left\{-\left(\frac{(\mathbf{k}+\mathbf{G})^2-Q_{BTP}^{2}}{2\sigma_{BTP}}\right)^2\right\}\right]\\
 &+& \frac{\partial\det\hat{s}}{\partial s_\nu}\left(E_{local} + E_{non-local} + E_{hartree} + \sum_\sigma\int_V d\mathbf{r} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{r})\rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{r}) + \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\rho_{core;\sigma}(-\mathbf{G})\right)\\
 &+& \frac{\partial\det{\hat{s}}^{-1}}{\partial s_{\nu}}E_{xc}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{G}}\frac{\partial V^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\rho(\mathbf{-G}) - \frac{4\pi}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}\rho(\mathbf{G})\rho(\mathbf{-G})\frac{G_i}{\mathbf{G}^4}\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_{\mathbf{G}}\left(\frac{\delta f_{xc}}{\delta |\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}\frac{d|\nabla\rho^a_\sigma|}{d\nabla\rho^a_\sigma}\right)(-\mathbf{G}) i\frac{\partial \mathbf{G}}{\partial s_\nu} \rho^a_\sigma(\mathbf{G})\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2\Omega}\sum_\sigma\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{xc;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial\rho_{pcc;total}(-\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_\mathbf{G} V_{total;\sigma}(\mathbf{G})\frac{\partial Q_{p,q}^{\tau}(\mathbf{G})}{\partial s_\nu}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} \Gamma_{\tau,p;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[D_{p,q}^{\tau;scr} - \epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right]P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q} P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast}\left[D_{p,q}^{\tau;scr} - \epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}Q_{p,q}^{\tau}\right]\Gamma_{\tau,q;\sigma,n;\nu}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &-& \frac{\partial\Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\frac{1}{N_{cell}}\sum_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\epsilon_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}\sum_{\tau,p,q}P_{\tau,p;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}\ast} Q_{p,q}^{\tau} P_{\tau,q;\sigma,n}^{\mathbf{k}}\\
 &+& \frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial \Omega^{-1}}{\partial s_\nu}\left[\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\frac{4\pi}{\mathbf{G}^2}e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} + \bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2\lim_{\alpha\rightarrow 0}\frac{4\pi}{\alpha^2} - \bigg(\sum_{\tau}Z_{\tau}\bigg)^2 4\pi\gamma^2 \right] \\
 &-&\frac{1}{\Omega}\sum_{\mathbf{G}\ne 0}|S^Z(\mathbf{G})|^2\left[\frac{1}{G^2} + \gamma^2 \right]\frac{4\pi}{G^2} e^{-\gamma^2\mathbf{G}^2} G_i\frac{\partial G_i}{\partial s_\nu} \\
 &-& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau'\ne\tau,\mathbf{R}}Z_{\tau}Z_{\tau'}\bigg[\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) + \frac{1}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\bigg] \times \\
 & & \frac{\tau_i-\tau'_i-\mathbf{R}_i}{|\tau-\tau'-\mathbf{R}|^2}\frac{\partial (\tau_i-\tau'_i-\mathbf{R}_i)}{\partial s_\nu}\\
 &-& \frac{1}{2}\sum_{\tau,\mathbf{R}(\mathbf{R}\ne 0)}Z_{\tau}^2\bigg[\frac{1}{\gamma\sqrt\pi}\exp\bigg(-\frac{|\mathbf{R}|^2}{4\gamma^2}\bigg) + \frac{1}{|\mathbf{R}|}\mathrm{erfc}(\frac{|\mathbf{R}|}{2\gamma})\bigg] \frac{\mathbf{R}_i}{|\mathbf{R}|^2}\frac{\partial\mathbf{R}_i}{\partial s_\nu}
\end{eqnarray*}

\section{Exchange Interaction}

\begin{equation}
E_{exchange} = -\frac{1}{2N_{cell}}\sum_{\sigma}\int\int\frac{1}{r_{12}}\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_1,\mathbf{r}_2)\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_2,\mathbf{r}_1)d\mathbf{r}_1d\mathbf{r}_2
\end{equation}
\begin{eqnarray*}
\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_1,\mathbf{r}_2) &=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n} f_{\mathbf{k},n} \Psi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_1)\Psi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_2)^\ast\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n} f_{\mathbf{k},n} e^{i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{r_1}}u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_1)e^{-i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{r}_2}u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_2)^\ast\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n} f_{\mathbf{k},n} e^{i\mathbf{k}\cdot(\mathbf{r_1}-\mathbf{r}_2)}u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_1) u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_2)^\ast\\
\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_1,\mathbf{r}_2)\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_2,\mathbf{r}_1) &=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'} e^{i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot(\mathbf{r_1}-\mathbf{r}_2)}u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_1) u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_2)^\ast u_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{r}_2) u_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{r}_1)^\ast\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'} e^{i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r_1}}u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_1) u^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{r}_1) e^{-i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot \mathbf{r}_2} u^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_2) u_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{r}_2)\\
e^{i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r_1}} u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_1) u_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{r}_1)^\ast &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'} \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}') e^{i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G}' + \mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r}_1} \\
e^{-i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot \mathbf{r}_2} u_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{r}_2)^\ast u_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{r}_2) &=& \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'} \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}') e^{-i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G}' + \mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r}_2}
\end{eqnarray*}
\begin{eqnarray*}
 & & \int\int\frac{1}{r_{12}}\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_1,\mathbf{r}_2)\rho_1^{\sigma,\sigma}(\mathbf{r}_2,\mathbf{r}_1)d\mathbf{r}_1d\mathbf{r}_2 \\
 &=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'}\int\int\frac{1}{r_{12}}\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'} \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}') e^{i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G}' + \mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r}_1} \\
 & \times & \frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega} \sum_{\mathbf{G}'',\mathbf{G}'''} \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}'')\phi_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}''') e^{-i(\mathbf{G}''-\mathbf{G}''' + \mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r}_2} d\mathbf{r}_1 d\mathbf{r}_2\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'}\frac{1}{N_{cell}^2\Omega^2} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'} \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}') \sum_{\mathbf{G}'',\mathbf{G}'''} \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}'')\phi_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}''') \\
&\times & \int\int\frac{1}{r_{12}} e^{i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G}' + \mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r}_1} e^{-i(\mathbf{G}''-\mathbf{G}''' + \mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot\mathbf{r}_2} d\mathbf{r}_1 d\mathbf{r}_2\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'}\frac{1}{N_{cell}^2\Omega^2} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'} \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}') \sum_{\mathbf{G}'',\mathbf{G}'''} \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}'')\phi_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}''') \\
&\times & \int\int\frac{1}{r_{12}} e^{i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot (\mathbf{r}_1-\mathbf{r}_2)} e^{i(\mathbf{G}-\mathbf{G}' - \mathbf{G}'' + \mathbf{G}''')\cdot\mathbf{r}_1} e^{i(\mathbf{G}''-\mathbf{G}''')\cdot(\mathbf{r}_1 - \mathbf{r}_2)} d\mathbf{r}_1 d\mathbf{r}_2\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'}\frac{1}{N_{cell}^2\Omega^2} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}'} \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G} - \mathbf{G}') \sum_{\mathbf{G}'',\mathbf{G}'''} \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}'' + \mathbf{G}''')\phi_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}''') \\
&\times & \int\int\frac{1}{r_{12}} e^{i(\mathbf{k}-\mathbf{k}')\cdot (\mathbf{r}_1-\mathbf{r}_2)} e^{i(\mathbf{G}' - \mathbf{G}'')\cdot\mathbf{r}_1} e^{i\mathbf{G}''\cdot(\mathbf{r}_1 - \mathbf{r}_2)} d\mathbf{r}_1 d\mathbf{r}_2\\
&=& \sum_{\mathbf{k},n,\mathbf{k}',n'} f_{\mathbf{k},n}f_{\mathbf{k}',n'}\frac{1}{N_{cell}\Omega} \sum_{\mathbf{G},\mathbf{G}',\mathbf{G}'''} \phi_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G})\phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G} - \mathbf{G}') \phi^\ast_{\mathbf{k},\sigma,n}(\mathbf{G}' + \mathbf{G}''')\phi_{\mathbf{k}',\sigma,n'}(\mathbf{G}''') \\
